```markdown
# Yuan Ze University Regulations for Recruiting Students of Master/Doctoral Program And On-job Students of Master Program

Passed by the 2nd Student Recruitment Committee of the 2012 School Year, October 5, 2011   
Authorized via the letter of the Ministry of Education under Tai-Kao-1-Tzu 1000205638, November 16, 2011   
Authorized via the letter of the Ministry of Education under Tai-Chiao-Kao-(4)-Tzu No.1060103311, July 20, 2017   
Passed by the 8th Student Recruitment Committee of the 2017 School Year, July 31, 2017

## Article 1 Establishment:

Yuan Ze University Regulations for Recruiting Students of Master/Doctoral Program And On-job Students of Master Program (hereafter, “these regulations”) are provided pursuant to Article 24 of University Act as well as Article 19 of its Enforcement Rules.

## Article 2 Student Recruitment Committee:

While processing matters relating to the recruitment of students of Master/Doctoral program and On-job students of Master program, the University shall establish Student Recruitment Committee (hereafter, “the Committee”) and process all matters based on the principles of equity, justice and openness. The committee shall be established according to “Yuan Ze University Organizational Rules of Student Recruitment Committee”.

## Article 3 Methods of admission:

1. Methods of admission for recruiting graduate students of a doctoral program include admission through recommendation, admission through examination, and direct admission into doctoral program.

2. Methods of admission for recruiting graduate students of a master program include admission through recommendation and admission through examination.

3. The admission for recruiting on-job graduate students of a master program will be based on admission through recommendation.

## Article 4 Quota of admission:

1. The admission quota for various academic programs and classes shall comply with the regulations regarding“Standards for Student Admission Quotas and Resources at Institutions of Higher Education” promulgated by the Ministry of Education, and be reported to Ministry of Education for approval.

2. The classes under various academic programs may be grouped upon authorization of the Ministry of Education, and may also be grouped separately to meet the needs for teaching and conducting researches. Examination subjects and admission quota for classes under various academic programs shall be specified in student recruitment regulations.

3. In the case of vacancy or insufficient admission, the quota may be re-allocated. The re-allocation principles shall be defined in the student recruitment regulations as the followings:

(1) The admission quota of each group (including that by enrollment status) of different

departments/institutes shall not be re-allocated.

(2) The admission quota of different groups of the same department/institute may be re-allocated based on the principle: the quota vacancies left from an earlier recruitment may be re-allocated to the later recruitment.

(3) The admission quota of the same group (other than that by enrollment status) of the same department/institute may be allocated discretionarily within the total admission quota.

4. While planning the quota of admission for recruiting students of Master/Doctoral program, it shall be processed based on the following rules:

(1) Quota of admission for recruiting students of Master/Doctoral program shall include regular students as well as on-job students; both quota shall be specified respectively.

(2) The number of students of Master/Doctoral program accepted through the recommendation process shall not exceed 60 percent of the total admission quota for each department/college/institute permitted by the Ministry of Education for that academic year.

## Article 5 Qualifications of admission:

1. Qualifications of admission for master/doctoral programs and on-job master programs shall be enacted pursuant to Article 23 of “University Act”, “Standards for Recognition of Equivalent Qualifications for University Entrance Examination”, as well as relevant provisions regulated by the Ministry of Education.

2. Examinees with foreign degrees shall meet the qualifications specified in provisions governing recognition of foreign diplomas: “Regulations Regarding the Assessment and Recognition of Foreign Academic Credentials for Institutions of Higher Education”, “Regulations Governing the Examination and Recognition of Educational Qualifications from Hong Kong and Macao”, “Regulations Regarding the Assessment and Recognition of Academic Credentials from the Mainland Area”, or Article 9 of “Standards for Recognition of Equivalent Educational Levels for University Admission”.

## Article 6 Admission criteria:

1. The Committee shall determine the minimum enrollment standard of each department/institute (group) before publishing the list of successful candidates. Examinees who get total scores beyond the minimum enrollment standard and fall within the admission quota shall be enrolled as admitted students; the others shall be identified as candidates on the waiting list.

2. If the number of examinees whose total grades meet the minimum enrollment standard is less than the admission quota, a statement of reasons may be submitted to the Committee to explain why the quota is not filled up and no candidates will be on the waiting list.

3. If more than two admitted students have the same total grade, the order of being admitted shall be subject to the same-score comparison measure for special enrollment stipulated in student recruitment regulations. If the same-score comparison measure fails to determine the order of being admitted, extra quota of admission may be accepted.

4. The vacancies remaining upon admitted students' completion of the registration, if any, may be filled by the candidates on the waiting list within the specific time limit. For students who apply for Master programs through the recommendation process, said time limit shall not be later than the day when the second semester begins as identified in the University's calendar. For students who apply for other programs or through other processes, said time limit shall not be later than the day when the school begins as identified in the University's calendar at the semester of the academic year of the enrollment.

5. When number of admitted student exceeds the admission quota, if necessary, it shall be approved by the Committee; the meeting minutes and related documents shall be handled in the following manners:

(1) If it is necessary to admit students more than the quota because of the same scores, this case shall be reported to and verified as well by the Ministry of Education within two weeks after the enrolling semester begins which is specified in the University’s calendar.

(2) If it is necessary to admit students more than the quota because of the University's administrative negligence, an admission review report shall be submitted to the Ministry of Education for approval within one month after confirming the existence of facts and then the additional students may be admitted upon approval of the Ministry of Education.

6. The admission list shall be reviewed and published by the Committee.

## Article 7 Schedule of recruitment:

1. Doctoral program: The process of recruitment shall be left to the University’s discretion.

2. Master program: Admission through recommendation process shall be held during the first semester of each academic year; admission through examination process shall be held during the second semester of each academic year.

3. On-job master program: The recruitment shall be held during the second semester of each academic year; it may be moved up to the first semester if necessary, but it can be done only once during each academic year.

4. The enrollment channels for various academic programs shall not conduct the enrollment by gradation of the admission quota.

## Article 8 Avoiding conflicts of interests, keeping grading materials or audio/video tapes

1. The examination affairs personnel shall be obligated to keep the examination affairs confidential. No one related to the examinee within three degrees of kinship is permitted to take part in examination affairs for avoiding conflicts of interests; anyone found to do so must be withdrawn from these examination affairs. keep the examination affairs in confidence.

2. If the examination for admission into an academic program is conducted in the form of oral test, field test or practical work, the process shall be sound recorded, video recorded or detailed in written. The written record shall be completed before the Committee decides the admission list. In the case that examinees may be marked with unusually high or low grades, detailed explanations shall be given on the grading documents.

3. All grading information shall be preserved for one year. If any examinees disagree with the grading and file an appeal, the relevant grading information shall be preserved until conclusion of the appeal or administrative remedy procedure.

## Article 9 Score review:

1. Examinees having objections to their test scores may apply for score review in accordance with the prescribed timeframes and procedures specified in student recruitment regulations.

2. Examinees shall not request to duplicate or regrade their answer sheets or test evaluation sheets. For each written and field test, examinees shall be allowed to apply for score review once only.

3. If there are mistakes found during score review which cause the change of scores, the order of being admitted shall be reranked based on the re-marked results; applicants shall not raise any objection.

4. If re-marked results of the score review turn out to reach the minimum requirements for acceptance, the applicants shall be admitted.

5. If re-marked results of the score review fail to reach the minimum requirements for acceptance, the applicants shall be disqualified from being admitted accordingly, and applicants shall not raise any objection.

## Article 10 Examinees’ appeals:

1. Examinees may file an appeal to the Committee with statements and reasons for the appeal along with documentary evidence if they have any complaints about recruiting affairs within fifteen days after the date of notification of the result to which it relates. Any appeal filed after the time limit will not be accepted. After receiving the appeal, the Committee shall make a reply within a month. The Committee may form a dedicated taskforce to process the appeal fairly if necessary. The Committee may advise the complainant of any related administrative remedies.

2. Resolving procedures for disputes over recruitment affairs shall be processed according to “Yuan Ze University Regulations Governing Appeals of Examinees”.

## Article 11 Other proceeding matters:

1. Government funded students and persons who bear the obligation for internship or service (military service) (e.g., government funded students of teacher preparation programs, students of military/police schools, active army and policemen, et al.) who apply for enrollment into the master or doctoral program of the University shall file the application in accordance with relevant regulations established by competent authorities. Students who are deprived of their qualifications due to the above-mentioned regulations shall be deemed as voluntary withdrawal; the University will not retain the admission qualifications of these students.

2. The application and verification for “Direct Admission into Doctoral Program” shall be processed according to relevant regulations.

3. Whether overseas Chinese, Hong Kong and Macao students, and foreign students who do not possess an Alien Resident Certificate or Permanent Resident Certificate can apply for on-job master programs shall be governed by respective regulations.

4. Places for attending courses: Places for attending courses shall be the campuses and branches set up by the University or verified by the Ministry of Education except for the case approved as a special project that is not subject to the restriction (a course established by the University which meets the specific regional needs with well-prepared teaching resources and facilities and there isn’t any relevant college department established in that same region).

5. Flexible courses and schedules are planned specifically to meet the special needs of on-job students of the master program. However, on-job students shall not take the same course with regular daytime students of a master program as a combined class except for the case with approval from all the regular daytime students in that course. The University reserves the right to decide whether to print the degree title “on-job program’ on the diploma or not.

6. The income and expenditures of recruitment affairs shall be handled in accordance with the University’s applicable regulations for accounting.

7. Matters not specified herein shall be governed by other relevant provisions and the University’s regulations.

## Article 12 The announcement and content of student recruitment regulations:

1. Student recruitment regulations shall be announced within 20 days prior to acceptance of the application or registration, at latest.

2. Student recruitment regulations shall specify in details about the departments offering admission, prescribed duration of study, admission quota, qualification of admission, exam subjects, exam dates, registration procedures, scoring criteria, admission criteria, allocation rules for admission quota, the same-score comparison measure, check-in procedures, rules for filling vacancies, score review, procedures for disputes over recruitment affairs, and other relevant regulations.

## 3. Qualifications of admission:

(1) Rules for whether the examinees shall graduate from the relevant departments/sections they intend to enroll.

(2) Rules for whether the examinees applying for on-job programs shall hold the seniority or work experience for the relevant departments/sections in nature. Rules for how the work experience and seniority shall be counted.

## 4. Examination subjects:

(1) Examinations for each academic program can be held through written test, oral test, written review field test, or practical work.

(2) The examination subjects and admission criteria of the on-job students shall be set according to their characteristics separately; their working experience and accomplishment shall be taken into consideration.

(3) Examination subjects, grading criteria, the percentage that each grade counts for the total score of each academic program shall be established by

department/college/institute, approved by the Committee, and specified in student recruitment regulations.

5. Student recruitment regulations shall specify in details about the same-score comparison measure and the rules for filling quota vacancies of each academic program.

6. Student recruitment regulations shall specify in details about the rules and qualifications for students to apply for enrolling into the University one semester earlier (including students admitted into a doctoral program, a master program through recommendation process, or an on-job master program).

7. Students who have been admitted into the University shall submit required certificates and relevant documents specified in student recruitment regulations when they go through the registration process.

8. Student recruitment regulations shall expressly state any matters related to examinees' interest and right. If necessary, such matters shall be marked in bold letters and enumerated by example to remind examinees and avoid any misunderstanding.

Article 13 These regulations will be adopted by Student Recruitment Committee before being reported to the Ministry of Education for ratification and implementation, as shall amendments when they are made.
```

```markdown
Article 1 In order to provide students with another opportunity to choose appropriate areas of study and attract more outstanding students to Yuan Ze University formulate this principle. Article 2 The quotas for each department (the quotas for each major in the Bachelor's program of the School of Management are allocated by themselves, and the actual quota is based on the official quota of the current year). The main application is to provide 15% of the department’s enrollment quota (unconditionally rounded up after the decimal point), for freshmen from other departments to apply. For freshmen who enroll in the 112th academic year (inclusive), their free transfer quotas will be allocated by each department. At least 5% of the enrollment quota, but no more than 10% of the transfer quota (unconditional admission after the decimal point), for first-year students from other departments to apply. Freshman applicants who apply to transfer majors can choose to fill in two choices per student. Article 3 Students who choose the same department as their first choice for transferring to another department will be admitted if their average academic performance in the first and second semesters of the original department reaches 60 points or above in both semesters of the current academic year. If the number of applicants does not exceed the transfer quota provided by the department; When the number of applicants exceeds the quota, the admission candidates shall be decided by the departmental meeting of each department. Article 4 For students who choose the same group of departments as their second choice for department transfer or who apply to transfer to a different group of departments, their application for transfer is not guaranteed by the quota. The method of transfer shall be in accordance with the school's department transfer regulations. Article 5 For first-year students who apply for free transfer to departments, the Academic Affairs Office will set a schedule for the application. Students will directly contact the department to apply. After the application list is reviewed by the departmental meeting of each department, the Academic Affairs Office will announce the admission list. Article 6 These principles shall be implemented after being approved by the Academic Affairs Meeting, and the same shall apply when revised.

# Yuan Ze University Regulations for Accepting Freshmen Transferring Freely

Passed by the 4th Student Recruitment Committee of the 100 School Year, on March 7, 2012   
Passed and Revised by the 3rd Student Recruitment Committee of the 106 School Year, on November 15, 2017   
Passed and Revised by the 7th Student Recruitment Committee of the 110 School Year, on June 1, 2012

If any controversies or disputes occurred regarding clauses of the contract, it shall always refer to its Chinese version.
```

```markdown
# Yuan Ze University Regulations for Recruiting Students of Industrial Technology Master Program

Passed by the 4th Student Recruitment Committee of the 2013 School Year, December 19, 2012   
Approved for future reference by Ministry of Education in Letter Tai-Kao-4-Tzu No.1020025481E, February 25, 2013

Article 1 Yuan Ze University (hereafter, ‘the university’) shall process matters relating to student recruitment on industrial technology master program based on relevant regulations. These regulations are provided pursuant to ‘Regulations Regarding the Assessment of Industrial Technology Master Programs’, Article 24 of University Act as well as Article 19 of its Enforcement Rules.

## Article 2 Composition of Student Recruitment Committee

Student Recruitment Committee for Industrial Technology Master Program is established to process matters relating to the recruiting affairs of industrial technology master program. The composition and tasks of the committee shall be in accordance with ‘Yuan Ze University Organizational Rules of Student Recruitment Committee’.

## Article 3 Student Recruitment Regulation

Student Recruitment Regulations shall include the followings: industrial technology master program offered, admission quota, years of the program, qualifications and requirements, examination date, examination subjects, grading of test results, admission criteria, resolving procedures for disputes over recruitment affairs, documents required, provisions related to the rights and responsibilities between industry-academic cooperation, rules for taking an examination, rules for reviewing the grades, procedures of registration and other related information. Student Recruitment Regulations shall be announced at least twenty days before the date accepting the sign-up. Stipulations of recruitment concerning the interests of the examinees shall be specified in Student Recruitment Regulations.

## Article 4 Admission methods

1. The method of student recruitment on industrial technology master program will be independent recruitment held by its department twice of a school year, spring semester and fall semester. Student recruitment for the spring semester shall be held beginning from September to December; student recruitment for the fall semester shall be held beginning from March to June.

2. Students on industrial technology master program shall be full-time students instead of being recruited as on-job students.

## Article 5 Admission quota

The number of students accepted shall not be counted into the total admission quotas permitted by the Ministry of Education. The number of students for each class shall not exceed thirty students.

## Article 6 Admission qualifications

1. Examinees who have graduated with a Bachelor’s degree from a domestic accredited university or from an independent institution that meets the criteria for overseas university or independent institution set by the Ministry of Education; or students who have the equivalent education qualification.

2. Examinees with foreign degrees shall meet the qualifications specified in provisions governing recognition of foreign diplomas in accordance with ‘Regulations Regarding the Assessment and Recognition of Foreign Academic Credentials for Institutions of Higher Education’. Examinees with overseas degrees shall meet the qualifications specified in provisions governing recognition of overseas diplomas.

3. To determine whether the departments originally majored by the examinees are compliant with the nature of the program they intend to enroll, the University shall specify it clearly in Student Recruitment Regulations.

4. To determine whether the military status of male examinees is qualified for admission into this program, the University and the cooperative industry shall have a discussion and the results shall be clearly specified in Student Recruitment Regulations.

## Article 7 Examining methods, subjects, percentage that each subject counts for

Examinations can be held through written test, oral test, written review, field test, practical work or aptitude test. Examination methods, percentage that each subject counts for, subjects of the written test, and numbers of the written test shall be established by the program, approved by Student Recruitment Committee for Industrial Technology Master Program, and specified in Student Recruitment Regulations.

## Article 8 Grading of test results

Matters relating to the grading of test results shall be processed based on the principles of equity, justice and openness. In the case that examinees may be marked with unusually high or low grades, detailed explanations shall be given on the grading documents. If the examination is held through oral test, field test or practical work, the process shall be audio taped, video taped or transcribed in details. The detailed transcript shall be finished before Student Recruitment Committee for Industrial Technology Master Program makes the final decision about the admission list. All documents relating to the grading of test results shall be retained for at least one year; all documents shall be retained till the termination of the appealing or administrative remedy procedure in the case that an appeal has been filed by an examinee.

Article 9 Admission criteria

1. Industrial technology master programs shall establish the minimum requirements for acceptance before the announcement of admission notification. These minimum requirements shall be approved by Student Recruitment Committee for Industrial Technology Master Program. Those examinees who meet the minimum requirements for acceptance and are top ranked within the admission quota shall be seemed as qualifiers; those who don’t shall be seemed as alternates on the waiting list. (If the number of examinees meeting the minimum requirements for acceptance is less than the admission quota, the vacancy may not be filled up and there are no alternates listed on the waiting list.) In the case that examinees get the same total score, the order of admission shall be subject to the method stipulated in Student Recruitment Regulations. In case of failure to determine the order of admission, a meeting shall be convened by Student Recruitment Committee for Industrial Technology Master Program to reach the resolution and make a final decision. Those examinees who don’t meet the minimum requirements for acceptance shall not be accepted even there is quota vacancy. The admission list shall be confirmed and officially announced by the committee. In the case the vacancy isn’t filled up due to the fact that the number of examinees meeting the minimum requirements for acceptance is less than the admission quota, the reasons (detailed explanations for the settings and rationalities of the minimum requirements for acceptance) shall be submitted to the committee for approval.

2. The number of employees working for the cooperative industry admitted into the program shall not exceed 40 percent of the admission quota.

3. Students being accepted shall register to the University before the deadline; students who fail to do so shall be regarded as giving up the acceptance and the quota vacancy may be filled up with alternates on the waiting list.

4. Students being accepted shall not apply for the maintenance of admission qualifications; those who don’t enroll in the appointed semester shall be deprived of their admission qualifications. Matters related to courses taking shall be processed in accordance with regulations of each program; above mentioned regulations shall be established separately.

5. Students being accepted shall be informed by the program with an admission notification and a contract specified the rights and responsibilities between industry-academic cooperation. Students shall sign a training contract with the cooperative industry while registering to the University.

6. In the special case of extra quota of admission, it shall be approved by Student Recruitment Committee for Industrial Technology Master Program; all the minutes from the committee along with relevant documents shall be reported to and verified as well by the Ministry of Education before the enrollment of accepted students. In the case that extra quota of admission is permitted due to administrative negligence, a review report for student recruitment affairs shall be submitted.

7. The rights and responsibilities between students and cooperative industry, and the punishment for breach of contract shall be clearly specified in Student Recruitment Regulations.

8. Accepted students who have enrolled into the program but apply for a suspension of study shall not be guaranteed for reinstatement of schooling and further employment.

## Article 10 Cases of counterfeited or impersonated documents

If the documents presented by examinees found to be forged, counterfeited, borrowing, impersonated or untrue, examinees who haven’t enrolled into the program shall be deprived of their admission qualifications; examinees who have enrolled into the program shall be ordered to withdraw from schooling and no academic records or documents shall be issued. If the situation is discovered after the student has graduated from the University or has been ordered to withdraw from schooling, the diploma or course certificate must be returned upon request and the qualification for graduation shall be revoked; students in this case shall be transferred to the prosecuting authority for legal treatment. Relevant regulations shall be clearly specified in Student Recruitment Regulations.

Article 11 The income and expenditures of industrial technology programs should be handled in accordance with the University’s applicable regulations for accounting. The expenditures of each program must not exceed its income.

## Article 12 Filing of an appeal

Examinees may file appeals if they have doubts about matters relating to recruiting affairs. Any appeal shall be made in written form and submitted to Student Recruitment Committee for Industrial Technology Master Program within a week of the date of receiving the test results. The case of appeal shall be replied by the committee within a month upon receipt of it. The committee may organize a team to go through a fair investigation when necessary and the appellants shall be informed of the administrative remedy procedure.

## Article 13 Examination affairs for attention

Recruitment team members in each program shall not be the ones who are related to the examinees within three degrees of kinship or those who are teaching in extension schools/institutes in order to keep the principles of interest avoidance. Regulations regarding the principles of interest avoidance shall be established separately. Any personnel engaged in handling examinations have the obligation to keep the examination affairs confidential.

Article 14 Matters not specified herein shall be governed by the university’s regulations and other

relevant provisions.

Article 15 These regulations will be adopted by Student Recruitment Committee before being reported to the Ministry of Education for ratification and implementation, as shall amendments when they are made.
```

```markdown
# Yuan Ze University

Passed by the 2nd Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2013, on November 06, 2013

1. The establishment of implementation guidelines for collaborative teaching of industry experts (hereafter referred to as the Implementation Guidelines) aims to reinforce the connection between university education and industry, offer students seamless knowledge of the industry science and technology, and cultivate applied talents suitable for enterprise’s needs.

## 2. Curriculum planning:

(1) Courses are classified as:

(a) Core courses- taught by Full-time faculty

(b) Practical/technical training/advanced courses- taught by industry experts alone or co-teaching with full-time faculty

(c) Elective courses- taught by Full-time or part-time faculty

(2) Department should keep up with the trend of the times and development orientation to open related courses or Seminars.

(3) Courses taught by industry experts must be approved by department, college and university curriculum committee.

(4) Department should define a rational ratio of courses taught by industry experts.

3. The qualification of industry expert should be examined by Teachers’ Evaluation Committee.

4. The Implementation Guidelines are passed by the Academic Affairs Meeting and implemented afterwards. The same procedure will be repeated for each revision.
```

```markdown
# Yuan Ze University Regulations Governing the Establishment of Y.Z. Scholarship

Amended and Adopted at the 9th Administrative Council of Academic Year 2014 on 2014.12.10 Amended and Adopted at the 20th Administrative Council of Academic Year 2014 on 2015.04.29 Amended and Adopted at the 2nd Administrative Council of Academic Year 2015 on 2015.08.26 Amended and Adopted at the 4th Administrative Council of Academic Year 2015 on 2015.09.23 Amended and Adopted at the 9th Administrative Council of Academic Year 2015 on 2015.12.02 Amended and Adopted at the 16th Administrative Council of Academic Year 2015 on 2016.04.13 Amended and Adopted at the 3rd Administrative Council of Academic Year 2016 on 2016.09.07 Amended and Adopted at the 9th Administrative Council of Academic Year 2016 on 2016.11.30 Amended and Adopted at the 19th Administrative Council of Academic Year 2017 on 2018.05.23 Amended and Adopted at the 12th Administrative Council of Academic Year 2018 on 2019.01.23 Amended and Adopted at the 22nd Administrative Council of Academic Year 2018 on 2019.07.17 Amended and Adopted at the 5th Administrative Council of Academic Year 2020 on 2020.10.07 Amended and Adopted at the 2nd Administrative Council of Academic Year 2022 on 2022.08.17 Amended and Adopted at the 12th Administrative Council of Academic Year 2022 on 2023.01.04 Amended and Adopted at the14th Administrative Council of Academic Year 2024 on 2025.04.16

Article 1 Yuan Ze University founder Mr. Y. Z. Hsu developed the Regulations to provide scholarship to Yuan Ze University students with academic excellence.

Article 2 The eligibility and amount of admission scholarship or living allowance for baccalaureate programs and master programs (excluding executive master programs) are described below:

1. Students admitted to Yuan Ze University baccalaureate programs via university personal application, university recommendation and screening test or entrance examinations shall be granted for paying their first-year tuition and miscellaneous fees equivalent to those of a national university standard when their performances at the College Entrance Exam in the subjects of Chinese, English and Mathematics finished at the upper half (75%) of all examinees. The aforementioned students who rank top 3 places at class in the academic performance of first year, receiving 80 points in the assessment of personal conduct without receiving grants for overseas exchange funds shall be granted for paying their tuition and miscellaneous fees equivalent to those of a national university standard, too, from the second to the fourth year of enrollment.

2. Graduates of Yuan Ze University students will be granted a grant equivalent to the tuition of one academic year in the first year of admission to the master’s program of the University.

3. Graduates of Asia Eastern University of Science and Technology students will be granted a grant equivalent to one academic year’s miscellaneous charges in the first year of admission to the master’s program of the Yuan Ze University.

4. Non-staff personnel at Yuan Ze University (including university-contracted staff, unit funded personnel, and project personnel), as well as full-time and contracted employees (including contracted assistant personnel) at Far Eastern Memorial Hospital, will be granted a grant equivalent to one academic year’s miscellaneous charges in the first year of admission to Yuan Ze University’s master’s program.

5. The grant, however, may suspend upon the decision of a department (college) affairs meeting approved by the YZU Scholarship Committee considering poor performance of the recipient or other reasons.

6. The amount of aforementioned scholarships shall be determined by the resolution adopted by the review from the Scholarship Committee.

Article 3 The guidelines related to Yuan Ze University doctoral programs (not include of DBA, college of management) admitted with exemption of tuitions are described below:

1. Students with ROC citizenship admitted to the Yuan Ze University doctoral program admission test (including screening test and bachelor/ master’s degree studying directly for doctoral degree) and do not have full time job (who must sign an affidavit letter) shall be exempt for tuition from the first to third year.

2. In case the students of doctoral programs have full-time job, show poor performance or other factors during the period of tuition exemption, as determined by the department (college) affairs meeting, the students will be reported to the Scholarship Committee for approval of reference to cancel the right of tuition exemption.

Article 4 The regulations governing the application and requisition for doctoral financial aids are described below:

1. New students admitted to the doctoral program will be approved at the college meetings for the list of Y.Z. Hsu doctoral student financial aids recipients in the amount of NT15,000 per month, for one to three years, according to the quota allocated for the current academic year. In particular, NT10,000 is a special scholarship and NT5,000is the research fundsfor teachers.

2. . Doctoral students receiving this financial aid must sign a statement. In case the students hold full-time job during the collection of this financial with proved investigation, Yuan Ze University may claim all scholarships collected during the full-time period and the students will be reported to relevant departments for disciplines.

3. In case the students show poor performance or other factors during the period of collecting the financial aid, as determined by the department (college) affairs meeting, the students will be reported to the Scholarship Committee for approval of reference to cancel the financial aids.

Article 5 The regulations governing the eligibility and amount for applying enrolling student excellence scholarship are described below:

1. Sophomore to senior students from the baccalaureate program having previous academic-year performance ranked in the top 3 places of their class, at least 80 points in conducts while the number of credits taken from previous academic year is at least 32 credits (inclusive) shall be distributed with scholarship of NT10,000 for the first place, NT8,000 for the second place, and NT6,000 for the third place. Unfilled vacancy for students meeting eligibility for certain reasonmay not be refilled.

2. Second-year students of master programs (excluding executive master programs) having previous academic-year performance ranked top 5% or first place per department (degree programs) while the number of credits taken from previous academic year is at least 12 credits (inclusive) and the average GPA of that academic year is at least 80 points (inclusive), shall be distributed scholarship in the amount of NT8,000. Unfilled vacancy for students meeting eligibility for certain reason may not be refilled.

Article 6 Other related regulations are described below:

1. Students from baccalaureate programs conforming to provisions prescribed in Article 2 and Article 5 may apply for only one disbursement.

2. The application and review procedures shall conform to the “Yuan Ze University Y.Z. Hsu Scholarship Examination Rules”for processing.

3. Doctoral students studying for doctoral programs shall pay for the balance of tuition and miscellaneous fees for master program, starting from the semester of voluntary change to master programs.

4. Foreign students, overseas Chinese students and students from Mainland meeting the provisions prescribed in Article 2, 3 and 4, may apply for scholarship if they have not collected other university scholarship and financial aids for that academic year.

Article 7 The Regulations are enacted after the discussion by the Admission Committee with proposal to the Administrative Council for adoption. Any modifications made to the Regulations shall be made in accordance as such.
```

```markdown
# Yuan Ze University Yu-Ziang Scholarship Review Regulations

March.24.2003, Approved by the 13th Executive Council Meeting of 2002 Academic Year.

May.21.2003, Approved by the 4th Student Affair Committee Meeting of 2002 Academic Year.

December.13.2006, Approved by the 1st Student Affair Committee Meeting of 2006 Academic Year.

April.21.2010, Approved by the 3rd Student Affair Committee Meeting of 2009 Academic Year.

May.09.2012, Approved by the 3rd Student Affair Committee Meeting of 2011 Academic Year.

December.10.2014, Approved by the 9th Executive Council Meeting of 2014 Academic Year.

April.20.2015, Approved by the 6th Admissions Committee Meeting of 2014 Academic Year.

July.29.2015, Approved by the 9th Admissions Committee Meeting of 2014 Academic Year.

September.26.2016, Approved by the 1st Admissions Committee Meeting of 2016 Academic Year.

May.10.2019, Approved by the 3rd Scholarship Review Committee Meeting of 2018 Academic Year.

November.06.2019, Approved by the 1st Scholarship Review Committee Meeting of 2019 Academic Year.

April.14.2023, Approved by the 2nd Scholarship Review Committee Meeting of 2022 Academic Year.

April.09.2026, Approved by the 2nd Scholarship Review Committee Meeting of 2025 Academic Year.

Article 1 To award scholarships to outstanding undergraduate and graduate students, these review regulations are established in accordance with Article 6 of the "Yuan Ze University Academic Scholarship Establishment Methods" (hereinafter referred to as the Establishment Methods).

## Article 2 The application and disbursement procedures are as follows:

1. Students who meet the eligibility criteria set out in Article 2 of the Establishment Methods should submit their application forms and relevant academic records within two weeks after the start of the academic year, following the announcements made by their respective departments or equivalent units. This scholarship is applied for once per academic year and is disbursed in two installments, one each semester.

2. Students who meet the eligibility criteria set out in Articles 3 and 4 of the Establishment Methods should submit an application form each semester during their first to third academic years.

3. Students who meet the eligibility criteria outlined in Article 5 of the Establishment Methods should apply according to the regulations.

4. If an applicant withdraws from the university during the academic year, any disbursed funds will be reclaimed, and their eligibility for this scholarship is forfeited without objection. Students who take a leave of absence may retain their eligibility for up to one year upon approval by the Scholarship Review Committee.

## Article 3 The review standards are as follows:

1. Students who meet the first criterion of Article 2 in the Establishment Methods will be reviewed based on the original copy of their college entrance examination

results by their departments, which will also submit a photocopy for reevaluation by the Scholarship Review Committee.

2. For students meeting the second and third criteria of Article 2 in the Establishment Methods, proof of scholarship eligibility is based on photocopies of graduation certificates from their respective schools.

3. For students who meet the fourth criterion of Article 2 in the Establishment Methods, proof of eligibility for this scholarship shall be based on the original employment certificate issued for that semester.

4. For second- to fourth-year students applying under the first criterion of Article 2 in the Establishment Methods, the review principles shall follow those set out in the first criterion of Article 5.

rticle 4 Each college completes the preliminary review according to the above regulations, compiles a list detailing the amounts to be disbursed, and submits it to the Student Affairs Office for consolidation. After reevaluation by the Scholarship Review Committee and approval by the Dean of Student Affairs, the Accounting Office will disburse the funds.

Article 5 Students who are entitled to the benefits specified in the first criterion of Article 3 of the Establishment Methods are limited to six semesters.

Article 6 These regulations shall be implemented following approval by the Scholarship Review Committee, and the same applies to amendments.

In case of any discrepancy between the Chinese and English version, the Chinese version shall prevail.
```

```markdown
# Yuan Ze University Regulations for Handling Violations of Academic Ethics

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting of the 2014 School Year, July 1, 2015   
Amended by the 3rd Academic Affairs Meeting of the 2017 School Year, January 10, 2018   
Amended by the 4th Academic Affairs Meeting of the 2021 School Year, March 2, 2022

Article 1 Yuan Ze University (hereafter, ‘the University’) hereby formulates these regulations in accordance with Article 7, Paragraph 2 of the “Degree Conferral Act” and Article 13 of “Yuan Ze University Regulations for Master and Doctoral Degree Qualifying Examination” to deal with students’ (current students and graduates included) violations of academic ethics.

Article 2 A violation of academic ethics means any of the following situations that happen during a student’s period of study:

1. Forgery: A student forged nonexistent application information, research data, or research results.

2. Falsification: A student used false application information, research data, or research results.

3. Plagiarism: A student used other people’s application information, research data, or research results without citing the sources. If a student fails to cite sources properly and the outcome is deemed unacceptable , the failure will be considered plagiarism.

4. Self-plagiarism: A student used the text from his or her own publications in the research project or thesis/dissertation without notation.

5. Duplicated without notation: A student repeatedly presented the same academic research result or publication without any proper indication.

6. Ghostwriting: Thesis/dissertation, application of a project, or research results were written by someone not involved.

7. Improperly influence the review of a thesis/dissertation by illegal or improper means.

8. Any other matter constitutes a violation of academic ethics.

Article 3 The type of conduct that constitutes plagiarism, forgery, fraud, or other unethical behaviors shall be investigated, reviewed, and determined by an investigation team made up of members appointed by the college involved.

Article 4 Reporting and filing complaints regarding violations of academic ethics, whether through educational authorities forwarding public grievances or by other means, shall specifically identify the violator of the report, provide detailed facts, attach evidence, and submit to the Office of Academic Affairs with the informant’s real name and contact address. After confirming with the informant that the reported matter indeed corresponds to the submitted complaint, then the case shall be immediately accepted for further action. Reports or complaints will not be accepted unless the violator is clearly identified and there are concrete facts with sufficient evidence. The identity of the informant and violator shall be kept strictly confidential.

Article 5 After receiving reports regarding violations of academic ethics, the Office of Academic Affairs shall determine whether to activate the case or not based on its conformance to the formal requirements of a report within three workdays of receipt. If the report in question does not conform to the formal requirements stipulated herein, the Academic Dean may close the case by notifying the informant in writing. As to the case whose formal requirements are deemed valid, the Academic Dean shall require the college with which the violator is affiliated to form an investigation team within ten days, conduct the review process in secrecy, and issue a resolution within two months. The aforementioned review period may be extended by up to one month if necessary.

Article 6 The investigation team shall be formed by the college with which the violator is affiliated, with the College Dean to be the convener; members of the team shall be appointed by the college and approved by the President. The investigation team shall consist of five to seven members including the College Dean, full-time faculty of the college, and impartial scholars or experts in law or a relevant professional field from within or outside of the University; scholars or experts outside of the University shall not be less than one-fourth of all the members. In the event of a conflict of interest between the College Dean and the violator, the Academic Dean shall serve as the convener instead. If a conflict of interest exists for both the College Dean and Academic Dean, the President of the University shall appoint a dean of another college to serve as the convener.

Article 7 Members of the investigation team shall recuse themselves from the process if they are involved with the violator in any of the following situations: 1. Being within the third degree of kinship by blood.

2. Being spouses, or within the third degree of kinship by marriage, or having had such a relationship.

3. Having had a dissertation/thesis advisor advisee relationship.

4. Being related through academic collaboration.

5. Being interested party.

6. Being those whose avoidance is required in accordance with other regulations.

7. Being individuals for recusal as proposed by the violator (not more than two).

Article 8 The violator shall be notified by the investigation team in writing to provide a written statement by the stipulated deadline or attend the team meeting to provide a statement in person. Failure to respond within the stipulated period or attend the meeting in person shall be deemed a voluntary forfeiture of their right to a statement.

In the event of degree conferral, the investigation team may require the presence of the violator’s advisor during a meeting if necessary.

Article 9 Every meeting the investigation team convenes shall be attended by at least half of all members to review a case. A concrete resolution shall be issued by the investigation team following the review process; the determining that the student violated academic ethics can be passed only with at least twothirds of the members attending and at least two-thirds of those attending concurring in their opinions. The review report and meeting minutes shall be submitted to the Office of Academic Affairs and the President for approval, after which both the informant and the violator shall be notified of the results. If a violator has any objection after receiving the notification of the review results, he or she may present a statement in written form stating all concrete facts and file a reapplication to the Office of Academic Affairs within thirty days. The reapplication can be filed only once. When dealing with a reapplication, the original resolution can be altered only with at least two-thirds of the members attending and at least two-thirds of those attending concurring in their opinions.

Article 10 Punishment and guidance for violations of academic ethics:

1. If enrolled students of the University are determined, through the review process, to have violated the academic ethics stipulated in Article 2 of these regulations, the department (college, institute, degree program)

shall submit the results and minutes of the review meetings to the Office of Student Affairs. The Office of Student Affairs shall then administer appropriate disciplinary actions in accordance with the student disciplinary regulations of the University.

2. If enrolled students or graduates of the University are determined to have violated the academic ethics stipulated in Article 2 of these regulations, and the violation is deemed severe by the investigation team, the violator’s degree shall be revoked and the invalidation of the violator’s diploma shall be publicly announced. After making the public announcement, the University shall notify the violator to return the degree diploma and shall inform other junior colleges, universities, and relevant institutions (agencies) of the circumstances of the revocation and invalidation. The University shall also send an official letter to National Central Library and the University’s library to notify them that the digital and hard copies of the violator’s dissertation/thesis shall be removed from the library collection. If the violation has not reached the level of degree revocation, the investigation team may implement appropriate measures for the violator. The advising professor may refer the case to the relevant college, department affairs meeting or Teacher Evaluation Committee for further deliberation.

3. If enrolled students of the University are determined to have violated the academic ethics stipulated in Article 2 of these regulations, they will be required to enroll in at least twenty units of relevant academic research ethics courses on the Center for Taiwan Academic Research Ethics Education (AREE) online teaching platform, starting from the date of the meeting with an issued resolution. They must obtain proof of course completion before being eligible to submit their graduation applications. The course completion certificate cannot be used for applying for degree examinations.

Article 11 After the investigation team determines that the case cannot be established, if the informant reports the same violator again, the complaint will not be accepted unless there is new evidence. When new evidence is confirmed, the case may be reviewed by the original investigation team.

Article 12 Matters not specified herein shall be governed by other relevant provisions of the Ministry of Education and of the University.

Article 13 These regulations will be adopted by Academic Affairs Meeting before ratification and implementation, as shall amendments when they are made.

The English translation is for reference only. In case of any discrepancy between Chinese version and English version, the Chinese version shall prevail.
```

<!-- OCR_END -->

```markdown
# Yuan Ze University Regulations for Students Suffering Difficulty in Their Schooling As A Result of A Disaster

Approved by the 1st Academic Affairs Meeting of the 2015 School Year, September 30, 2015   
Approved by the 8th Academic Affairs Meeting of the 2023 School Year, May 1, 2024

Article 1 The school in order to protect the rights and interests of students affected by major disasters, has formulated these regulations based on the Ministry of Education's " Direction for Junior College and Higher Levels to Deal With the Rights of Education of Student Affected by Major Disaster Rights of Education" and Article 64-1 of YZU Study Regulations.

Article 2 The following regulations shall be applicable to students suffering difficulty in their schooling as a result of a disaster.

Article 3 Students suffering difficulty in their schooling as a result of a disaster referred to in the regulations shall be recognized by the educational authority.

Article 4 Entrance Examination and Registration:

1. Students who register for the entrance examination will be provided with venue support services by the school; if unable to attend, they may apply for a refund.

2. Students admitted to the school through various entrance examinations may complete the registration process by mail and submit the required supporting documents for follow-up procedures. They may also authorize someone else to handle the related tasks on their behalf.

Article 5 Students who fail to return to school with expiration of the deferment may be granted for an extension of one more year on a case-by-case basis.

Article 6 Regulations for Student Course Selection and Attendance Methods:

1. The required minimum credits taken for each semester are not applicable to students referred to in the regulations.

2. Students who take courses below the requirement shall paycredit fees for the courses they take.

3. Students with special needs for taking courses nearby may be actively contacted by the school to coordinate cross-campus course enrollment. Additionally, depending on the individual case, they may be exempt from restrictions on course availability and credit limits.

4. Under the premise of ensuring the quality of student learning, the school may implement flexible measures to assist students in taking courses through synchronous, non-blended distance learning.

5. The school may, taking into consideration the students' physical and mental adaptation and learning needs, assist in retaining their eligibility for dual degree programs, research, exchange opportunities, or participation in industry-academia cooperation projects abroad.

1. Students who apply for a leave of absence during the semester are not subject to the restrictions on applying after the start of the final exams. They are also not required to pay the relevant tuition and fees. If fees have already been paid, the school may refund the corresponding tuition and fees.

2. Students who fail to return to school with expiration of the suspension for two years may be granted for an extension of two more years on a case-by-case basis.

3. Students who withdraw from the semester are not subject to restrictions on the timing of their withdrawal, and the school may refund the relevant tuition and fees.

4. Students who have reached the maximum study period but are still unable to complete the required course credits may be granted a special extension of their study period for an additional two years.

## Article 8 Regulations on Student Leave of Absence, Grade Assessment, and Credit Transfer:

1. Students may apply for leave of absence by mail (or by personally logging into the leave system) and submit the required supporting documents for follow-up procedures. They may also authorize someone else to handle the related tasks, without being subject to the restrictions on absences, deductions in exams, or compulsory suspension regulations.

2. The school may adjust the grading method based on the nature of the course, and handle course grades through make-up exams or other remedial measures. The make-up exam grades will be calculated based on the actual performance.

3. The school may relax the credit limits for courses that students apply to transfer or exempt.

4. The school may taking into consideration the student's physical and mental condition, assist in transferring to an appropriate department for study.

## Article 9 Adjustment of Student Graduation Requirements:

1. The school may adjust the course content and study hours of courses (such as internships, physical education, and service learning) based on the nature of the subjects, as deemed appropriate.

2. The school may relax the graduation requirements for students (such as English tests, certification exams, etc.) and provide alternative solutions.

Article 10 The school should understand the actual needs of students in terms of physical and mental adaptation, academic learning, and career counseling. It should refer them to relevant units in a timely manner to provide the necessary resources and assist them in overcoming major disasters.

## Article 11 These regulations are adopted by Academic Affairs Meeting, as shall amendments when they are made.
```

```markdown
# Yuan Ze University

# Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights

Passed at the 3rd 2015 Academic Affairs Meeting on January 20, 2016   
Passed at the 21st 2016 Administration Meeting on June 14, 2017   
Passed at the 26st 2021 Administration Meeting on July 20, 2022   
Proposed at the 11st 2021 Administration Meeting on December 21, 2022

## Article 1

The Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights (hereafter referred to as “the Highlights”) is established to help faculty members and students foster the proper ethical awareness and attitude toward research.

## Article 2 The Highlights are targeted at the following:

2.1 Graduate (including executive graduate) and postgraduate students enrolled starting from the academic year of 2016

2.2 Full-time professors and researchers employed starting from the academic year of 2017 (including special assistant and adjunct assistant).

2.3 Full-time professors employed before the academic year of 2017 who have not applied for a National Science Technology Council (NSTC) Project from the National Science Technology Council (hereinafter called the “NSTC”).

## Article 3 The Highlights are implemented as follows:

3.1 The university’s Office of Academic Affairs shall upload all student information to the website of the Center for Taiwan Academic Research Ethics Education after the add/drop period in the first semester of each academic year to facilitate student account creation. Department administrators are responsible for the creation and management of student accounts during this semester. The Personnel Office is responsible for collecting the relevant information of newly employed professors and researchers and submitting the information to the Office of Research and Development to create teacher accounts.

3.2 Faculty members and students shall access the Center for Taiwan Academic Research Ethics Education through the university website and complete the Academic Research Ethics Education Program (hereafter referred to as “the Program”) in the first semester of employment or enrollment.

3.3 Faculty members and students who have completed the compulsory Program and passed subsequent learning evaluation can apply for and download a certificate of completion from the website.

## Article 4

Students receiving the Program are required to pass an online learning evaluation and submit the completion certificate to their department administrator to apply for the oral examination of dissertation. Students failing the evaluation are required to receive and pass a re-evaluation before applying for their oral examination, and will not be eligible for oral examination without completing the Program.

Article 5 Principal investigators and all research participants listed in the submitted research proposal who are first-time applicants for a NSTC Project are required to complete no less than six hours of the Program and submit a valid certificate to the Office of Research and Development within three

years prior to the date of application.

Participating researchers (including special assistant and adjunct assistant) who was employed for the first time to implement the NSTC Project after the implementation of the plan, within three months from the date of employment, submit the relevant supporting documents of the six-hour Academic Research Ethics Education training course to the Office of Research and Development.

## Article 6

Teachers who conduct lectures on academic ethics related topics in combination with the course can subsidize the lecture hour fee; The application procedures, the number of subsidy and the amount will be announce by the Office of Research and Development according to the budget allocated for current year.

Article 7 The Highlights and all subsequent amendments shall take effect once approved in the Administration Meeting.
```

```markdown
# Yuan Ze University Regulations Governing Diversity Instruction Curriculum Review

Adopted at the 18th Administrative Council of Academic Year 2015 on

2016.05.11

Amended and Adopted at the 23th Administrative Council of Academic

Year 2016 on 2017.07.12

Amended and Adopted at the 26th Administrative Council of Academic

Year 2021 on 2022.07.20

## Article 1 icle1

In conformance with the purpose of effective integrating university diversity instruction resources, improve diversity instruction activities and promote diversity instruction function, Yuan Ze University has developed the “Yuan Ze University Regulations Governing Diversity Instruction Curriculum Review” (hereinafter referred to as the Regulations).

Article 2 To promote diversity instruction curriculum that must be reviewed by Tier III Curriculum Committee includes the follows: Distance learning course, MOOCs course, co-instruction course, and maker courses, where instructors submit application to the department offering the courses in one semester in advance and shall be reviewed in accordance with the meeting schedule and procedures of Curriculum Committee.

Article 3 The tasks of curriculum commits at all tiers are described below:

3.1. The department offering the course will conduct the substantive review on the diversity instruction curriculum of the university.

3.2. Upgrade the quality of university diversity instruction activities and promote the development, design, review, and follow-up matters of instructional functions.

3.3. Mastering of other matters related to the development of diversity instruction resources.

rticle 4 Curriculum adopting diversity instructional approach will be reviewed and approved by Tier III Curriculum Committee before receiving additional pay. Meanwhile the same course applying for multiple diversity instructional approaches will be disbursed by the best hourly wage item. Additional hourly pay can be applied for deducting instruction hours. Project promotion (such as overseas programs, 3+1 exchange students, etc.) courses offered in special classes are not subject to the provision of these regulations.

The principles of diversity instruction curriculum review and standards of hourly wage disbursement are described below:

4.1 Digital learning courses aims to utilize digital learning resources, using internet as the interface with encourage more students to focus on personal interests and demand in acquiring the latest knowledge online anytime, anywhere. Moreover, students’ learning effect will be improved to accommodate educational adaptive instruction, including the follows:

4.1.1. Distance learning course shall conform to the regulations governing the regulation of applying Yuan Ze University distance learning course offer. First course offer will be given 0.5 times additional pay while non-first course offer will be given 0.5 times additional pay but may not re-apply for large-class additional pay.

4.1.2. The additional pay for hourly wage of MOOCs courses will be calculated by physical courses and distance learning courses separately. At most 0.5 times additional pay will be given to distance learning courses while the additional pay for distance learning courses is calculated as follows: distance learning courses over 4 weeks will be given 0.3 times additional pay. Distance learning courses over 6 weeks will be given 0.4 times additional pay. Distance learning courses over 8 weeks will be given 0.5 times additional pay. The number of students taking previous distance learning courses will be applied as the important consideration for the departments to evaluate and determine if to continue offer the course. MOOCs courses must be offered on offcampus public platforms and shall be announced to all university before the class begins.

Due to the pre-class design and production requirement, digital learning course offered for the first time may be applied for one-deduction of pre-course design in one semester prior to the design and production with review and approval by the Tier III Curriculum Committee. Each instruction is restricted to one class per semester. In case the following semester applied for deduction is not offered, the instructor shall make up for the one hour of instruction previously applied for deduction.

## 4.2 Co-Instruction:

4.2.1 The instruction hours of co-instruction courses shall be calculated for hourly wage by the hours of actual instruction given by the instructors and shall be calculated up to 2 times. Co-instruction instructors will need to jointly instruct in class in person and the application shall describe the principal instructor and collaborating instructor, the weeks of in-class instruction for the co-instruction courses, course innovation and necessity of co-instruction for key consideration of review.

4.2.2 The hours when the teacher arrives at the class but has no actual teaching hours shall not be counted as hours.

## 4.3 Maker Courses:

Maker courses aim to develop students with capacities in hands-on experience, innovation and actual problem-solving. The courses will be given 0.3 additional pay. Instructors shall guide students with software or hardware creation and practice in person. The ownership of Maker course works shall be specified by the curriculum committee of department offering the course and shall reach agreement between the students and instructors before the class begins. A public outcome presentation should be held at the end of the term to announce the entire university for purpose of observation.

Article 5 The curriculum committees at all levels may invite the instructors to attend the meeting and present a report.

Article 6 The result of promoted diversity instruction curriculum review will not affect subsequent course offer. Nonetheless courses without adoption may not be disbursed with additional diversity instruction pay.

Article 7 The Regulations are enacted after the adoption and announcement by the Administrative Council. Any modifications made to the Regulations shall be made in accordance as such.
```

```markdown
# Key Points for Yuan Ze University English Proficiency Exam Rewards

2016 Jul 06 Passed in 22nd Executive Council Meeting 104 academic year   
2024 FEB 21 Passed in the 13th Executive Council Meeting 112 academic year

1.In order to enhance the English proficiency of undergraduate students at Yuan Ze University, the “Procedures for Yuan Ze University English Proficiency Exam Rewards” (referred to as “these procedures” below) are especially established.

2.Undergraduate students at Yuan Ze University (referred to as “the university” below) who participate in the specified exams during their academic tenure and meet the reward criteria as outlined in these procedures will be granted a reward by the university as an encouragement.

## 3.Qualified Applicants:

(A)Undergraduate students admitted from the 105 academic year (2016) onwards (excluding any English program majors and the Department of Applied Foreign Languages) who participate in the specified exams during their freshman and sophomore years and meet the application requirements.

(B)Regarding freshmen, their eligibility begins from August 1st of the current academic year.

4.The “specified exams” in Article 2 of these procedures and the criteria for granting rewards are as follows：

## 5.Application Steps:

(A)Following the announcement of these reward regulations, applicants who meet the application criteria must submit an application form, their student ID card (original and copy), and their score transcript (original and copy). The application period is before November 30th in the first semester and before May 31st of the second semester. Rewards will be issued once per semester.

(B)Applicants should submit transcripts within six months from the date the transcript is issued. If the issuance date is not indicated on the transcript, the examination date indicated on the transcript will be used as the basis for calculation.

6.To ensure fairness, only students with active enrollment status can apply during their academic tenure; individuals are limited to one application. Applicants who submit applications after the deadline will be considered for the following semester’s application. As for applicants who are in their sophomore year and submit applications after the sophomore-year second-semester deadline, if the date of the score acquisition falls within their sophomore year, their application documents may be considered for the following semester.

7.These guidelines have taken effect since they were approved in the university Executive Council Meeting. The process will be the same for any amendments.
```

```markdown
# Yuan Ze University Regulations for Students of International Bachelor Programs Applying for Change of Major

Passed by the 1st Academic Affairs Meeting of the 2017 School Year, September 27, 2017   
Amended by the 7th Academic Affairs Meeting of the 2019 School Year, June 17, 2020   
Amended by the 1st Academic Affairs Meeting of the 2023 School Year, September 27, 2023

Article 1 “Yuan Ze University Regulations for Students of International Bachelor Programs Applying for Change of Major” is provided to offer students of International Bachelor Programs a flexible and wide range of learning channels.

Article 2 Students of International Bachelor Programs who are not interested in the current major to which they are enrolled may apply for a change of major after they have completed their first academic year of studies. Each student can only apply one time. Each department may establish its own criteria for reviewing applications.

Article 3 Students of the same College who want to apply for transferring into International Bachelor Programs shall meet all the criteria set forth by the program. The International Bachelor Program will select the best students for admission.

Article 4 Students who apply for a change of major into or out of International Bachelor Programs shall file an application during the $2 ^ { \mathrm { n d } }$ semester of each academic year.

Article 5 Application procedures:

1. Students applying t for a change of major into or out of International Bachelor Programs shall fill out an application form, which must be signed and approved by the applicant’s parents or guardians (except for students who meet the legal age requirement of adulthood under the Civil Code). The application form shall be submitted to Registration Division of Office of Academic Affairs along with the applicant’s personal development plan and transcript of the previous semesters. These documents will then be sent to the corresponding department for reviewing and approval.

2. Based on the reviewing results of the corresponding department, students may be required for a grade repetition due to their ability levels; those who don’t accept the requirement will be deemed as to waive the application.

3. The review results shall be approved by the meetings of accepting departments and sent to Office of Academic Affairs to process the change of an applicant’s student status which shall be based on the applicant’s order of department preference. The change of an applicant’s student status will be effective beginning from the next semester after the application.

Article 6 Matters not specified herein shall be governed by “Yuan Ze University Regulations for Change of Major”.

Article 7 These regulations shall be implemented following the approval of the Academic Affairs Meeting, modifications shall follow the same procedure.
```

<!-- OCR_END -->
