```markdown
# Yuan Ze University Independent Enrollment Regulations for Project-Based Admission of Overseas Taiwanese Students Returning to the ROC to Complete Studies Due to Severe Pneumonia with Novel Pathogens

Passed by the 13th Student Recruitment Committee of the 2020 School Year, May 20, 2020

Authorized via the letter of the Ministry of Education under Tai-Chiao-Kao-(4)-Tzu No.1090075098, May 26, 2020

Passed by the 2nd Student Recruitment Committee of the 2021 School Year, October 22, 2020

Authorized via the letter of the Ministry of Education under Tai-Chiao-Kao-(4)-Tzu No.1090155549, October 29, 2020

## Article 1

“Yuan Ze University Independent Enrollment Regulations for Project Based Admission of Overseas Taiwanese Students Returning to the ROC to Complete Studies Due to Severe Pneumonia with Novel Pathogens” (hereafter, ‘these regulations’) are provided by Yuan Ze University (hereafter, ‘the University’) pursuant to “University Act”, “Regulations Governing Academic Advancement Incentives for Students from Major Disaster Areas”, as well as “University/College Processing Project Based Admission of Overseas Taiwanese Students Returning to the ROC to Complete Studies Due to Severe Pneumonia with Novel Pathogens” (hereafter, ‘the Project Based Admission’) to process matters relevant to the admission of overseas Taiwanese students applying for daytime programs of bachelor, master and doctoral degrees.

Article 2 While processing matters relating to the admission of overseas Taiwanese students returning to the ROC to complete studies, the University shall establish Recruitment Committee for The Admission of Overseas Taiwanese Students (hereafter, ‘the Committee’) and process all matters based on the principles of equity, justice and openness. The committee shall review admission methods, admission quota, the University’s student admission information material, selection principles, the procedure for handling exam-related disputes, and other matters regarding the taking of an admission exam.

The regulations governing the formation of the Committee shall be prescribed separately.

Article 3 The admission is processed through independent enrollment, and admission methods can be held through written test, oral test, written review, field test, or practical work. The committee shall set relevant rules out clearly in its student admission information material.

If the admission is processed through oral test, field test or practical work, the process shall be tape-recorded, videotaped or recorded in writing; written records shall be completed before the Committee decides a roll of successful candidates. If any candidate has received an extremely high or low grade, concrete reasons shall be clearly stated in the scoring sheet.

Article 4 The Project-Based Admission shall make adjustments for recruitment target, admission quota, admission schedule, and any other compliance matters prescribed by the Ministry of Education.

Article 5 Admitted targets shall be limited to Taiwanese students who have been studying abroad and who meet regulatory requirements prescribed in The Project-Based Admission. Qualifications of admission shall be enacted pursuant to Article 23 of “University Act”, “Regulations Governing the Assessment and Recognition of Foreign Academic Records by Institutions of Higher Education”, “Regulations Governing the Examination and Recognition of Educational Records from Hong Kong and Macao”, “Regulations Governing the Assessment and Recognition of Academic Credentials from the Mainland Area”, and “Standards for Recognition of Equivalent Educational Levels for University Admission”.

Article 6 The Committee shall determine the minimum acceptance criteria for each department before a roll of successful candidates is announced. Candidates who have satisfied the minimum criteria and are within the additional admission quota will be accepted candidates, while others are wait-listed candidates. If the number of students of each department/degree program who meet the minimum requirements for acceptance is less than the additional admission quota, the quota may not be filled up, which shall be reported to the Committee with detailed explanations to get approval. In this case, there shall be no alternates listed on the waiting list. If there are any quota vacancies after the admission, the vacancy of additional quota may be filled up with alternates on the waiting list before the deadline specified in the University’s student admission information material. This deadline shall not be later than the day when the school begins as identified in the University's calendar for the certain admission year. For examinees with the same score, the order of admission shall be subject to the method stipulated in the University’s student admission information material. In the case that there are more than two examinees with the same total score, the Committee shall convey a meeting to reach the resolution and make a final decision. If more candidates are accepted than the additional admission quota due to the University's administrative negligence, the Committee shall convey a meeting to reach the resolution and make a final decision. The minutes of the meeting, relevant documents, and an admission review report shall be submitted to the Ministry of Education for approval within one month after confirming the existence of facts. The admission list for additional quota shall be confirmed and officially announced by the Committee.

Article 7 The University’s student admission information material shall specify the admission schedule, the admission methods, the departments offering admission, the prescribed duration of study, the admission quota, test registration requirements, exam subjects, exam dates, registration procedures, eligibility criteria, selection principles, the order of admission for examinees with the same score, rules for filling vacancies by wait-listed candidates, review of grades, check-in procedures, credit offsets, the procedure for handling exam-related disputes, and other matters regarding the rights and responsibilities of persons taking an entrance examination. The admission information material shall be approved by the Committee and be made public on the admission section of the University’s website not later than 20 days before the University begins to accept applications. The period for receiving registration shall not be less than seven days. The admission list for additional quota shall be officially announced before August 31, 2020. Admitted students shall enroll into the University at the first semester of academic year 2020.

The departments offering admission mentioned in the first paragraph shall be limited to the University’s current colleges, institutes, departments, subjects, and degree programs; departments under the control of student numbers by the government shall not process this project-based admission such as teacher education, medical school, Chinese medicine school, and dental school. Colleges, institutes, departments, subjects, degree programs of technical and vocational colleges and universities with the teaching quality checked by the MOE as subject to ongoing supervision or fail the review shall not process this project-based admission.

Article 8 The following tasks shall be carried out cautiously: making and printing of examination questions, correcting of individual answer sheets, sealing of the collected answer sheets, supervision of examinations, grading of examination scores, announcement of the list of successful examinees, and registration to the University. All grading information shall be preserved for one year. If any examinees disagree with the grading and file an appeal, the relevant grading information shall be preserved until conclusion of the appeal or administrative remedy procedure.

Any personnel engaged in the University’s examination affairs who is related to the examinee within three degrees of kinship shall not be permitted to take part in examination affairs for avoiding conflicts of interests; anyone found to do so must be withdrawn from these examination affairs. The personnel engaged in examination affairs shall be obligated to keep the examination affairs confidential.

Article 9 Examinees having objections to their test scores may apply in writing to the Committee for score review within the deadline stipulated in the University’s student admission information material. Officially written responses shall be made by the University within a week after the application.

Examinees may not request to duplicate or regrade their answer sheets or test evaluation sheets; for each subject, examinee shall be allowed to apply for score review once only. If there are mistakes found during score review which cause the change of scores, the order of being admitted shall be reranked based on the re-marked results; applicants shall not raise any objection. If re-marked results of the score review turn out to reach the minimum requirements for acceptance, the applicants shall be admitted. If re-marked results of the score review fail to reach the minimum requirements for acceptance, the applicants shall be disqualified from being admitted accordingly, and applicants shall not raise any objection.

Article 10 Examinees may file an appeal to the Committee with statements and reasons for the appeal along with documentary evidence if they have any complaints about admission affairs within ten days after the date of admission list being announced. After receiving the appeal, the Committee shall make official responses within a month. The Committee may form a dedicated taskforce to process the appeal fairly if necessary. The Committee may advise the complainant of any related administrative remedies.

Article 11 In the case that the examinees are caught cheating on the exam or the documents presented by examinees found to be forged, counterfeited, borrowing, impersonated or untrue, examinees who haven’t enrolled into the program shall be deprived of their admission qualifications; examinees who have enrolled into the program shall be ordered to withdraw from schooling and no academic records or documents shall be issued. If the situation is discovered after the student has graduated from the University, the diploma shall be revoked; the qualification for graduation shall be invalidated and be publicly announced.

Article 12 Matters not specified herein shall be governed by Yuan Ze University Study Regulations, other relevant provisions, and the University’s student admission information material.

Article 13 These regulations will be adopted by Student Recruitment Committee before being reported to the Ministry of Education for ratification and implementation, as shall amendments when they are made.
```

# Yuan Ze University Regulations for Change of Major for Graduate Students of Master/Doctoral Programs

Passed by the 7th Academic Affairs Meeting of the 2019 School Year, June 17, 2020   
Approved for future reference by Ministry of Education in Letter Tai-Kao-2-Tzu No. 1090105783, July 29, 2020   
Approved for future reference by Ministry of Education in Letter Tai-Kao-2-Tzu No. 1090122371, August 21, 2020

Article 1 These regulations are provided for processing matters relating to graduate students’ applications for a change of majors, departments, tracks or programs of study (hereafter, ‘a change of major’). These regulations are provided pursuant to Paragraph 1of Article 59 of “YZU Study Regulations”.

Article 2 Graduate students who are not interested in the current major to which they are enrolled may apply for a change of major. The application and admission dates each year accord with the University’s school calendar.

Article 3 Graduate students who meet all of the following criteria may apply for a change of major:

1. Students who have completed one semester of study;

2. Students with a Grade Point Average (GPA) of over seventy;

3. Students who meet the requirements set forth by the accepting departments.

Article 4 Application for a change of major shall be processed with the following procedures:

1. Graduate students who wish to change their majors shall complete the application form, and then submit along with their transcripts of the previous semesters and relevant documents to Registration Division of Office of Academic Affairs for preliminary examination by the deadline announced. Applications to change the current major shall be approved by the advising professor, the department chair and college dean.

2. Each department may establish its own criteria for reviewing applications for a change of major. The request shall be discussed and reviewed by the accepting departments. The review results shall be approved by the accepting department chair and college dean, submitted to Registration Division of Office of Academic Affairs, and then published upon approval of the Provost (Dean of Office of Academic Affairs).

Article 5 Each student can only apply one time. Students granted approval to change their majors shall not file for a change in or withdrawal of their application. They must fulfill the graduation requirements set forth by the accepting departments and meet the requirements for the length of time in which the study must be completed pursuant to “YZU Study Regulations”. The maximum length of study shall not be extended following a change of major. Disapproved applicants may continue to register in their current departments.

Article 6 Credits obtained from courses taken at the student’s previous major may be waived; students shall file an application for credit exemption in accordance with “Yuan Ze University Regulations for Credit Exemption” by the date stipulated in the University’s school calendar.

Article 7 Inter-division transfers within the same department/institute of a graduate school shall be processed in accordance with these foregoing regulations.

Article 8 Matters not specified herein shall be governed by relevant provisions of the Ministry of Education and the University.

Article 9 These regulations will be adopted by the Academic Affairs Meeting before being reported to the Ministry of Education for ratification and implementation, as shall amendments when they are made.
```

# Yuan Ze University Regulations Governing Admission of New Immigrants

Passed by the 9th Student Recruitment Committee of the 2021 School Year, April 22, 2021

Authorized via the letter of the Ministry of Education under Tai-Chiao-Kao-(4)-Tzu No 1100060752, May 21, 2021

Article 1 “Yuan Ze University Regulations Governing Admission of New Immigrants” (hereafter, ‘these regulations’) are provided by Yuan Ze University (hereafter, ‘the University’) pursuant to Article 24 of “University Act”, Article 19 of its “Enforcement Rules”, “Regulations for Criteria of Reviewing Recruiting Procedure of Universities”, as well as “Regulations Governing Admission of New Immigrants to Universities” to process the admission of new immigrants to the University’s doctoral program, master program (on-job students of master program included), or bachelor program (transfer not included).

Article 2 The University shall establish Recruitment Committee for Admission of New Immigrants (hereafter, ‘the Committee’) and process all matters relating to the admission of new immigrants based on the principles of equity, justice and openness. The committee shall review admission methods, admission quota, the University’s student admission information material, selection principles, the procedure for handling exam-related disputes, and other matters regarding the taking of an admission exam.

The regulations governing the formation of the Committee shall be prescribed separately.

Article 3 In these regulations, the term “new immigrants” refers to persons who have received approval to apply for naturalization in accordance with the provisions of Article 4, Paragraph 1, Subparagraphs 1 to 3 of the “Nationality Act” and lodged an application. New immigrants who are applying for admission to a university shall also submit a copy of their Permit Certificate of Naturalization and a copy of their letter giving permission to apply for naturalization, or other related documentary evidence that is sufficient to prove that they satisfy the eligibility criterion. If any of the documentary evidence has been lost or is impossible to submit, the person applying for admission may authorize the University to verify their eligibility; if an applicant’s documentary evidence has not been submitted and checked by the time they have to register at the University, their eligibility will be cancelled.

New immigrants who have the qualification of graduating from high school or meet the equivalent level of education may apply for the University’s bachelor program. Those who hold a bachelor degree or meet the equivalent level of education may apply for the University’s master program. Those who hold a master degree or meet the equivalent level of education may

apply for the University’s doctoral program.

New immigrants who hold overseas school credentials should be handled in accordance with the provisions of “Regulations Governing the Assessment and Recognition of Foreign Academic Records by Institutions of Higher Education”, “Regulations Regarding the Assessment and Recognition of Academic Credentials from the Mainland Area”, and “Regulations Governing the Examination and Recognition of Educational Qualifications from Hong Kong and Macao”.

Article 4 New immigrants may only register and enroll at a university in accordance with the provisions of the preceding article one time.

Article 5 The University’s quota for new immigrants who take part in the admission of first year students to that university by lodging an application for admission is in addition to the admission quotas for the colleges, institutes, departments, divisions, and degree programs. The additional admission quotas for new immigrants are calculated as being two percent of the respective admission quotas that the Ministry of Education has already approved for the colleges, institutes, departments, divisions, and degree programs at the University. If a calculation results in a number that includes a decimal fraction, the number will be rounded up to the next integer. The admission quota of each college, institute, department, division, and degree program shall not be re-allocated.

Article 6 The admission is processed through independent enrollment and shall be processed one time only.

Article 7 The admission guidelines shall be approved by the Committee and be made public not later than 20 days before the University begins to accept applications. The admission guidelines shall detail the departments offering admission, the prescribed duration of study, the admission quota, qualification requirements, exam subjects, exam dates, registration procedures, scoring criteria, methods of acceptance for admission, the ranking order of admission for examinees with the same final entry score, check-in procedures, rules about filling vacancies by wait-listed candidates, review of grades, the procedure for handling exam-related disputes, and other related rules. The admission guidelines shall expressly state any matters related to examinees' interest and right. If necessary, such matters shall be marked in bold letters and enumerated by example to remind examinees and avoid any misunderstanding.

Assessment methods may include written test, oral test, written review, field test, or practical work; the scores of General Scholastic Ability Test, Advanced Subjects Test, English Listening Comprehension Test, or Testing Center for Technological and Vocational Education shall not be used as admission criteria.

Scoring criteria and percentage of each mentioned assessment method shall be stipulated in the admission guidelines. If the examination is held through oral test, field test or practical work, the process shall be tape-recorded, videotaped or recorded in writing; written records shall be completed before the Committee decides a roll of successful candidates. If any candidate receives an extremely high or low grade, concrete reasons shall be clearly stated in the scoring sheet.

Article 8 Before a roll of successful candidates is announced, the Committee shall determine the minimum acceptance criteria for each college, institute, department, division, and degree program. The Committee shall rank the examinees’ scores. Candidates who have satisfied the minimum criteria and are included in the admission quota will be accepted candidates, while others are wait-listed candidates.

If the number of applicants meeting the minimum requirements for acceptance is less than the admission quota, the quota may not be filled up, which shall be reported to the Committee with detailed explanations to get approval from the Committee. In this case, there shall be no alternates listed on the waiting list.

If there are any quota vacancies after the new recruits enroll into the University, the vacancy may be filled up with alternates on the waiting list before the deadline specified in the admission guidelines. This deadline shall not be later than the day when the school begins as identified in the University's calendar at the semester of the academic year of enrollment.

In the case that there are more than two examinees with the same final entry score, the order of admission shall be subject to the method stipulated in the admission guidelines. If examinees have the same final entry score after having various criteria compared or being further evaluated in some other way, each of them shall be admitted without the University being subject to the additional admission quota of two percent of the approved quota, and the University shall report the circumstances to the Ministry of Education for future reference.

Article 9 After each recruitment unit at the University publicly announces its admission results, the University shall report the number of new immigrant applicants, the number who were admitted, and the number who then enrolled to the Ministry of Education for future reference.

## Article 10

All examination affairs shall be carried out cautiously while processing the admission of new immigrants. The examination affairs personnel shall be obligated to keep the examination affairs confidential. No one related to the examinee within three degrees of kinship is permitted to take part in examination affairs for avoiding conflicts of interests. All grading information shall be preserved for one year. If any examinees disagree with the grading and file an appeal, the relevant grading information shall be preserved until conclusion of the appeal or administrative remedy procedure.

Article 11 Examinees may apply for a review of grades or file an appeal within the deadline specified in the admission guidelines if they have any doubts about grading or recruiting affairs which violate their rights and interests. For any unsolvable problem after the processing of personnel in charge of admission affairs, an appeal shall be filed to the Committee with statements and reasons along with documentary evidence within twenty days after the following day of the roll of successful candidates is announced or informed; overdue will not be accepted.

After receiving the appeal, the Committee shall make a reply within a month and advise the appellant of any related administrative remedies. The Committee may form a dedicated taskforce to process the appeal fairly when necessary. Should a conflict of interest arise in the review process among any relevant parties of the Committee meeting, including a Committee member and the appellant, the principle of interest avoidance shall be adopted in accordance with the provisions of Article 32 of “Administrative Procedure Act”.

An appeal shall be filed in writing by the appellant.

The taskforce may, ex officio or upon the appellant’s request, allow the appellant and relevant parties to attend the meeting to give explanations when necessary.

An appellant may file an appeal to the Committee a maximum of once for the same matter. The chairman of the Committee shall inform the appellant in writing of the decision made after a review of the appeal.

## Article 12

In the case that the documents presented by new immigrant students found to be forged, borrowing, counterfeited, students who haven’t enrolled into the program shall be deprived of their admission qualifications; students who have enrolled into the program shall be ordered to withdraw from schooling and no academic records or documents shall be issued. If the situation is discovered after the students have graduated from the University, the diploma shall be revoked; the qualification for graduation shall be invalidated and be publicly

announced.

Article 13 Matters not specified herein shall be governed by relevant provisions of the Ministry of Education and the University.

Article 14 These regulations will be adopted by Student Recruitment Committee before the admission guidelines are announced and before being reported to the Ministry of Education for ratification and implementation, as shall amendments when they are made.
```

# Yuan-Ze University Regulations for Admission Video Interview

Passed by the 14th Student Recruitment Committee of the 2022 School Year, July 27th, 2022

1. At the time of the scheduled interview, candidates who are unable to return to the country or attend the interview in person at our school due to the following reasons may submit an application for a video interview with the provision of proof: a. living outside the island or being overseas due to study or work b. taking courses or internship abroad c. major illness and injury

d. major impacts of the pandemic: the University shall, in compliance with the orders issued by the competent authority pursuant to the Central Epidemic Command Center or the Ministry of Education, implement and adjust measures for people who are assigned by Central Epidemics Command Center to home quarantine, self-care for the prevention of COVID-19, home isolation, being reported as a suspected case before receiving the test results during the selfhealth management, or being the confirmed case of COVID-19 and are assigned to be quarantined/isolated.

2. At the time scheduled for the interview, the University may announce that ‘a video interview’ will be adopted instead of ‘an oral interview on campus’, in compliance with the orders issued by the competent authority or the Ministry of Education in response to the alert levels of pandemic. Candidates do not need to apply for the video interview, but they must sign "YZU Video Interview Test Guarantee Letter" and send it to the Department/Institute by e-mail/fax before the interview.

3. Candidates who meet the various requirements to apply for the video interview pursuant to the first paragraph must go to the University’s website for recruitment regulations to download and sign "YZU Video Interview Test Guarantee Letter" along with "YZU Application Form for Admission Video Interview" and send them to the Department/Institute by e-mail or fax one week before the interview day. Applications that fail to comply with the regulations will not be accepted, except for those who are affected by the pandemic mentioned in the fourth subparagraph of Paragraph 1 shall file a late application before the interview day.

4. If the application for a video interview is approved, the scheduled time will be arranged by the Department/Institute and the candidate will be notified by e-mail.

5. The Department/Institute and the candidate must conduct a connection test on the day before the formal video interview.

6. The connection test is conducted again 30 minutes before the start of the formal video interview; after the test is completed, the candidate must wait for the interview online.

7. During the formal video interview, candidates must cooperate with the presentation of the admission ticket and identification for verification. Those who do not submit the supporting documents will not be able to participate in the video interview and will be considered as being absent from the interview.

8. If the candidate fails to take the test on time for the official video interview, the interviewer shall wait for 5 minutes (with the time recorded through the screen capture); if the candidate is still not online after 5 minutes, it will be considered as being absent, and the candidate shall not request a make-up test.

9. Candidates must choose an appropriate venue for the video interview to ensure that the interview process is not interrupted. During the video interview, no other person shall be present, and the candidate must accept the instructions of the interviewer to use the camera to scan around the venue to prove it.

10. The entire video interview process is recorded with both video and audio, and the relevant data shall be kept for at least one year.

11. The video interview criteria, the number of interviewers, and the interview time must be consistent with the on-site interview.

12. If the candidate complains and proves that the interview cannot be conducted because of the University’s “intra-school network” failure, the interview may be conducted again.

13. In the case that the candidates are caught with using a false name or with other acts of cheating discovered during the interview with proof, candidates shall be deprived of their admission qualifications according to “YZU Regulations for Student Conduct in Recruiting Examinations”. Candidates who have enrolled into the program shall be ordered to withdraw from schooling in addition to the legal responsibilities involved; no diplomas shall be issued. If the situation is discovered after the student has graduated from the University, the diploma shall be revoked; the qualification for graduation shall be invalidated and be publicly announced.

14. Matters not covered herein shall be conducted in accordance with relevant regulations of the Ministry of Education.
```

## Yuan Ze University Regulations for Criteria of Reviewing Recruiting Procedure of Undergraduate Students through Selection

Passed by the 9th Student Recruitment Committee of the 2022 School Year, April 22, 2022

Article 1 “Yuan Ze University Regulations for Criteria of Reviewing Recruiting Procedure of Undergraduate Students through Selection” are provided pursuant to Regulations for Criteria of Reviewing Recruiting Procedure of Universities, as well as “Yuan Ze University Regulations for Admission of Undergraduate Students through Selection”. The reviewing of recruiting procedure which may include document review, an oral examination, or a written examination shall be subject to these regulations.

Article 2 All personnel engaged in examination affairs shall process matters relating to the recruitment of students based on student recruitment regulations and relevant regulations.

Article 3 The examination can be held through document review, interview, or written examination. For document review and interview, at least three (or above) members of the examination committee shall be involved. For written examination, at least two (or above) members shall be responsible for the setting of test questions for each examination subject.

Article 4 Due to special circumstances, each department (or class) may, with the approval of its departmental meeting, employ professors from other departments (or classes) or retired professors as document review committee members and interview committee members, but the members shall not exceed onethird of the total members of each program (or group). Members shall have the teacher qualifications issued by the Ministry of Education. Interview committee members shall participate in the entire interview process.

Article 5 The personnel engaged in examination affairs shall be obligated to keep the examination affairs confidential and avoid conflicts of interests under the following circumstances:

1. The appointed examination (including paper correction, document review, and interview) committee members who work in cram schools, or whose spouses and relatives related to the examinee within three degrees of kinship shall initiatively withdraw from examination-related affairs to avoid conflicts of interests.

2. The appointed supervisors or examination affairs staff whose spouses and relatives related to the examinee within three degrees of kinship shall initiatively withdraw from examination-related affairs to avoid conflicts of interests.

3. If the professors who serve as examination affairs staff or examination committee members for the current year have conducted simulated reviews or interviews for high school students, they shall

withdraw from the examination-related affairs. 4. Other related conflicts of interest. Document review and interview conveners shall strengthen the word and deed standards for the document review committee members and interview committee members as well, to avoid controversies caused by inappropriate words.

Article 6 Prior to document reviews, interviews, and written examinations, each department (or class) shall hold a preparatory meeting to discuss issues such as evaluation items, evaluation standards, and evaluation methods, and implement the principles of fairness and justice. The evaluation items and standards for document reviews and interviews in the preceding paragraph shall be formulated by each department (or class) before document reviews and interviews.

Article 7 If the examination is held through interview, field test or practical work, the process shall be taperecorded, videotaped or recorded in writing; written records shall be completed before the Student Recruitment Committee decides a roll of successful candidates. If any candidate has received an extremely high or low grade, concrete reasons shall be clearly stated in the scoring sheet. All documents relating to the grading of test results shall be retained for at least one year; all documents shall be retained till the termination of the appealing or administrative remedy procedure in the case that an appeal has been filed by an examinee.

Article 8 The personnel engaged in examination affairs (document review, interview, or written examination) shall be obligated to keep the examination affairs confidential.

Article 9 Matters not specified herein shall be governed by other relevant provisions made by the Ministry of Education.

Article 10 These regulations will be adopted by Student Recruitment Committee before being reported to the Ministry of Education for ratification and implementation, as shall amendments when they are made.
```

#### OCR 59: files/regulations/c%20en/1-89.pdf

```markdown
# Yuan Ze University Regulations Governing Determination of The Name of Degrees in Different Categories, Conferral of Degrees, and Alternatives to Submission of a Master's Degree Thesis or Doctoral Dissertation

Passed by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting of the 2021 School Year, March 30, 2022   
Approved for future reference by Ministry of Education in Letter Tai-Kao-2-Tzu No. 1110046489, May 23, 2022   
Passed by the 4th Academic Affairs Meeting of the 2022 School Year, March 1, 2023   
Approved for future reference by Ministry of Education in Letter Tai-Kao-2-Tzu No. 1120053227, June 17, 2023   
Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting of the 2023 School Year, January 3, 2024   
pproved for future reference by Ministry of Education in Letter Tai-Kao-2-Tzu No. 1130014184, February 29, 2024

Article 1 These regulations are established in accordance with “Degree Conferral Act”, “Regulations Governing Determination of The Name of Degrees in Different Categories, Conferral of Degrees, and Alternatives to Submission of a Master's Degree Thesis or Doctoral Dissertation”, “Yuan Ze University Study Regulations”, and “Yuan Ze University Regulations for Master and Doctoral Degree Qualifying Examination”.

## Article 2

Degrees conferred by Yuan Ze University refer to the bachelor’s degree, the master’s degree, and the doctoral degree. The requirement governing the conferral of degrees at all levels and categories shall be stipulated clearly by each department (institute, degree program, class, or group) with the followings to be taken into account: academic degree level, study period, required credits, internship requirement, graduation requirement, acquisition of core competency, professionalism, and requirement of various assessments. These requirements shall be stipulated by the curriculum committee of department (institute, degree program, class, and group) and submitted to the curriculum committee meeting and Academic Affairs Meeting before implement. The requirements for conferral of a master/doctoral degree may include a work, proof of achievement accompanied by a written report, a technical report, or a professional practice report instead of a thesis or a dissertation.

Article 3 The determination of Chinese and English names for various categories of degrees shall comply with international practices and trends, and refer to the reference manual for Chinese and English degree names published by the Ministry of Education. It shall also be based on the distinctive characteristics of each department, institute, or degree program, curriculum content, and the nature of the fields, whether they are academic or professionally oriented.

Article 4 The Chinese and English names for conferred degrees at all levels and categories shall be examined by each department (institute, degree program, class, or group) meeting and Academic Affairs Meeting before implement.

Article 5 The regulations governing Chinese and English names for conferred degrees at all levels and categories with the year of implementation, the criteria for conferral, and the awarding and registration of the associated degree diploma shall be complied by the Office of Academic Affairs and published on the University's website.

Article 6 A student undertaking a bachelor’s degree program who completes the required courses and credits within the prescribed time stipulated in the University’s Study Regulations, satisfies all the graduation requirements, passes examination and assessment with satisfactory results, shall be conferred a bachelor’s degree.

Article 7 A student undertaking a master's degree program who completes the required courses and credits within the prescribed time stipulated in the University’s Study Regulations, satisfies the graduation requirements and submits a thesis, passes the master degree examination, shall be conferred a master's degree.

A student who undertakes a master's degree program in the field of fine arts, design, applied science or technology, or sports may submit a work, proof of achievement accompanied by a written report, or a technical report instead of a master's degree thesis. A student who undertakes a master’s degree program in the field of professional practice may submit a professional practice report instead of a thesis.

The regulations governing the scope of such determinations pertaining to each suitable field referred to in the preceding two paragraphs for which a work, proof of achievement accompanied by a written report, a technical report, or professional practice report may be submitted instead of a thesis are allowed as follows:

1. Fine arts, design: A student whose works accompanied by written reports which can indicate the significant contributions his/she has made to theoretical analysis in the fields of music, opera, theater, theater arts, dance, folk arts, audio-visual arts, visual arts, new media arts, design, and other arts disciplines.

2. Applied science or technology: A student who has patent, technology transfer or innovation in the field of life sciences, environment, physics and chemistry, mathematics and statistics, information and communication, engineering, manufacturing, building and construction, agriculture, transportation, and other technological fields; a student whose case study has won awards in national or international technical competitions or contests; a student whose results accompanied by written reports which can indicate the significant contributions he/she has made to theoretical analysis in the fields of industry-academia cooperation, application and derivative of technology, or improvement projects.

3. Sports: In the field of leisure sports, competitive sports, and athletics, either the student or the athlete under his/her designated guidance participates in major national or international sports competitions, achieves notable rankings, and his/her proof of achievement accompanied by written reports which can indicate the significant contribution he/she has made to the field. The scope of the above-mentioned competitions shall be determined and announced by the competent authority.

4. Professional practice: This refers to research areas or content primarily focused on practical applications. A professional practice report refers to a research topic undertaken by a master's student that involves practical applications which emphasize the practical nature of the research content and may involve a research project or a short paper instead of an academic master's thesis.

The criteria for a work, proof of achievement accompanied by a written report, a technical report, or a professional practice report referred to in the preceding paragraphs and the required submission materials shall be determined by each department (institute, degree program, class, or group) with standards equivalent to an academic thesis or dissertation at that level. The criteria shall be passed by each department (institute, degree program, class, or group) meeting and Academic Affairs Meeting before being included in the regulations for degree completion requirements.

Article 8 A student undertaking a doctoral program who completes the required courses and credits, and passes the qualifying examination for doctoral candidates, may become a doctoral candidate.

A student undertaking a doctoral program who completes the required courses and credits within the prescribed time stipulated in the University’s Study Regulations, satisfies the graduation requirements and submits a dissertation, passes an examination conducted by a doctoral degree examination committee, shall be conferred a doctoral degree.

A student who undertakes a doctoral program in the field of fine arts, design, applied science or technology, or sports may submit a work, proof of achievement accompanied by a written report, or a technical report instead of a doctoral dissertation. The scope of such determinations shall be processed in accordance with the provisions of Article 7, Paragraph 4, Subparagraphs 1, 2, and 3.

The criteria for a work, proof of achievement accompanied by a written report, a technical report, or a professional practice report referred to in the preceding paragraphs and the required submission materials shall be determined by each department (institute, degree program, class, or group) with standards equivalent to an academic thesis or dissertation at that level. The criteria shall be passed by each department (institute, degree program, class, or group) meeting and Academic Affairs Meeting before being included in the regulations for degree completion requirements.

Article 9 The information in the form of a work, proof of achievement accompanied by a written report, a technical report, or professional practice report, which may be seen as a substitute for the master's thesis or doctoral dissertation mentioned in Article 7 and 8, may be submitted in paper, disk, CD, or other electronic storage media.

Article 10 The content of a work, proof of achievement accompanied by a written report, a technical report, or a professional practice report, which may be seen as a substitute for the master's thesis or doctoral dissertation mentioned in Article 7, Paragraph 2 and 3, shall include the followings:

1. Fine arts, design: Creation or performance concepts and case descriptions, theoretical foundations, interpretation and analysis of methods and techniques, contributions of works and achievements, and other derived accomplishments.

2. Applied science or technology: Concepts of research and development of technology, case descriptions, theoretical foundations, interpretation and analysis of methods and techniques, contributions of achievements, and other derived accomplishments.

3. Sports: Competition experience and case descriptions, theoretical foundations, interpretation and analysis of methods and techniques, contributions of achievements, and other derived accomplishments.

4. Professional practice: Concepts of professional practices, case descriptions, theoretical foundations, interpretation and analysis of methods and techniques, contributions of achievements, and other derived accomplishments.

Article 11 The content of the written report and technical report which may be seen as a substitute for the doctoral dissertation in Article 8, Paragraph 3 shall be regulated in accordance with the provisions of the preceding Paragraphs 1 to 3.

Article 12 Diplomas of various degrees shall include the information of a student’s name, date of birth, name of college, department, institute, degree program, date of graduation, degree name, and reference number.

Those who meet any of the following notes are eligible to have them recorded on the diploma and academic transcripts.

1. If a student applies for a reissue of a diploma, the date of reissue will be stated on the diploma.

2. For those who meet the requirements for obtaining a minor or double major degree at this University or another school, the name of the school and department shall beadditionally noted.

3. Those who meet the study requirements for the program professional courses of our school can add the major field and the name of the course studied on the degree certificate (excluding credit courses and cross-discipline courses)

Article 13 The date of degree conferring is January for the first semester and June for the second semester.

Bachelor students of delay graduation who have completed required courses and credits during the study period but do not meet the graduation requirements, and who have obtained relevant certificates and submitted applications during their studies, are not subject to the restrictions in the preceding paragraph. If the applicant in the preceding paragraph still has credits for other subjects that do not affect graduation, he must first complete the course suspension before applying.

Master's and doctoral students who have passed the degree examination and completed the submission of the thesis or dissertation, fulfilling the requirements for graduation in terms of prescribed courses and credits, will have their degree conferred in the month corresponding to the completion of graduation conditions.

The procedure of degree conferring will be handled according to the schedule announced by Office of Academic Affairs.

Article 14 The principles for the add and adjustment of college, department, institute, and degree program names, as well as the conferment of degree titles, as approved by the Ministry of Education, are as follows:

1. The adjustment of college, department, institute, and degree program names: Starting from the date of approval, the diplomas of its students shall include the new names of colleges, departments, institutes, and degree programs, as well as the conferred degree titles.

2. The suspension of student recruitment into college, department, institute, and degree program: If students receive assistance to transfer to related colleges, departments, institutes, or degree programs, they shall be conferred degrees according to the colleges, departments, institutes, or degree programs they transferred into, and this information shall be recorded on their degree diplomas.

3. The grouping of college, department, institute, and degree program: The grouping of enrolled students shall follow the procedures specified for the add and adjustment of department (institute), which require approval from the Ministry of Education; and this information shall be recorded on their degree diplomas. The grouping of enrolled students formed for instructional purposes shall not be recorded on their degree diplomas.

Article 15 In the case that the University revokes a degree in accordance with Article 9 of “Yuan Ze University Study Regulations”, Article 13 of “Yuan Ze University Regulations for Master and Doctoral Degree Qualifying Examination”, Article 10 of “Yuan Ze University Regulations for Handling Violations of Academic Ethics”, Office of Academic Affairs shall then notify the person involved to return the degree diploma and shall inform other junior colleges, universities, and relevant institutions (agencies) of the circumstances of the revocation and invalidation.

Article 16 Matters not specified herein shall be governed by “Yuan Ze University Study Regulations” and other relevant provisions.

Article 17 These regulations will be adopted by Academic Affairs Meeting before being reported to the Ministry of Education for ratification and implementation.

The English translation is for reference only. In case of any discrepancy between Chinese version and English version, the Chinese version shall prevail.
```

# Yuan Ze University Independent Enrollment Regulations for Admission of Students with Excellent Athletic Performance

Passed by the 4th Student Recruitment Committee of the 2023 School Year, November 30, 2022

Approved for future reference by Ministry of Education in Letter Tai-Chiao-Shou-Ti-Bu-Tzu No1120001828, January 16, 2023

Article 1 “Yuan Ze University Independent Enrollment Regulations for Admission of Students with Excellent Athletic Performance” (hereafter, ‘these regulations’) are provided by Yuan Ze University (hereafter, ‘the University’) pursuant to Article 24 of “University Act”, Article 19 of “Enforcement Rules of the University Act”, Article 19 of “Regulations on Facilitating Admission to Higher Education for Students with Excellent Athletic Performance at High School Level and Above”, and “Guidelines for Universities to Process the Tasks to Review Admission Regulations” to process matters relevant to the admission of students with excellent athletic performance.

Article 2 While processing matters relating to the independent admission of students with excellent athletic performance, the University shall establish the Student Recruitment Committee (hereinafter referred to as ‘the Committee’) based on “Yuan Ze University Organizational Rules of Student Recruitment Committee”. The Committee shall handle the affairs based on the principles of equity, justice, and openness and deals with urgent matters related to the admission.

The Committee shall process all matters such as admission quota, eligibility requirements for applicants, categories of sports, recruitment methods, exam subjects and the proportion of each subject's score in the total score, scoring criteria, the minimum requirement for admission, nomination of referee committee for evaluating the field test, and other matters regarding the admission affairs.

Article 3 The quota for independent admission is made according to the quota granted by the MOE and should be included in the total number of the admission quota verified by the MOE. The admission quota of each college, institute, department, division, and degree program shall not be re-allocated. If vacancies are left by independent admission of students with excellent athletic performance, they may be added to the quota for admission through the College Entrance Examination. Students who have been granted into the

University via this admission method shall not apply for the registration and placement admission of college entrance in the current school year; those who violate this regulation, their qualifications for admission to the University will be canceled.

## Article 4 Eligibility requirements for applicants:

Applicants must be graduates of or have graduated from a public (general or vocational) senior high school or a government-accredited private (general or vocational) one, or meet the requirements listed in “Standards for Recognition of Equivalent Educational Levels for University Admission”, and meet any of the following qualifications of excellent athletic performance:

(1) having the qualifications to be screened and selected through the admission exam, which are listed in the Regulations on Facilitating Admission to Higher Education for Students with Excellent Athletic Performance at High School Level and Above;

(2) having competed in any sports competitions at an international level as an athlete representing a country and obtained any certificates;

(3) having competed in any national sports games, citizens sports games, National High School Games, National Indigenous Games, and National Disabled Games and obtained any certificates;

(4) having competed in any league matches recognized by the Sports Administration of the MOE and any national tournaments held by any national sports associations and obtained any certificates;

(5) having been a member of a school team at a general or vocational senior high school for more than one year, competed in any games at a county/city level or above, and obtained any certificates or records of participation in the games;

(6) having been a graduate in a class of sports talent at a senior high school and obtained a certificate.

Article 5 The admission of students with excellent athletic performance may be processed through various assessment methods for each individual department of the University .The admission guidelines shall detail the departments offering admission, categories of sports, prescribed duration of study, admission quota, registration deadline, qualification requirements, exam subjects, assessment methods, proportion of each subject's score in the total score, exam dates, registration procedures, registration materials, scoring criteria, the ranking order of admission for examinees with the same final entry score, standards of acceptance for admission, review of grades, check-in procedures, rules about filling vacancies by wait-listed candidates, the procedure for handling exam-related disputes, and other related rules. The admission guidelines shall be submitted to the Committee for review and be announced 20 days before the admission is open for application. The admission guidelines shall expressly state any matters related to examinees interest and right. If necessary, such matters shall be marked in bold letters and enumerated by example to remind examinees and avoid any misunderstanding.

Article 6 Assessment methods may include written test, oral test, written review, field test, or practical work. If the exam is held through oral test, field test or practical work, the process shall be tape-recorded, videotaped or recorded in writing; written records shall be completed before the Committee decides a roll of successful candidates. If any candidate receives an extremely high or low grade, concrete reasons shall be clearly stated in the scoring sheet.

## Article 7 Standards of acceptance for admission:

(1) The Committee shall decide the minimum admission criteria for each sport category before releasing admission results. Candidates whose admission scores are above the entry score and who are within the admission quotas will be initially admitted students. Other candidates that are not listed as initially admitted students may be wait-listed. After initially admitted students report their willingness to enroll at YZU, the vacancies of admission quota can be filled by waitlisted candidates until the quota is full, and the deadline for filling up the vacancies shall not exceed the deadline stated in the admission guideline. The deadline shall not exceed the first school day (as stipulated on the school calendar) in the current semester of the academic year wherein the admitted students enroll..

(2) If the number of candidates meeting the entry score requirement is less than the admission quota of each department, institute, and degree program (group/division), each of the teaching units may admit a number of students below its quota upon approval by the Committee after it submits relevant reasons to the Committee for review. In such cases, no candidates will be wait-listed.

(3) This deadline shall not be later than the day when the school begins as identified in the University's calendar at the semester of the academic year of enrollment.

(4) In the case that there are more than two examinees with the same final entry score, the order of admission shall be subject to the method stipulated in the admission guidelines. If examinees have the same final entry score after having various criteria compared or being further evaluated in some other way, each of them shall be admitted without the University being subject to the additional admission quota of two percent of the approved quota, and the University shall report the circumstances to the MOE for future reference.

(5) The list of admitted students shall be submitted to the Committee for confirmation and can be formally announced after the Committee confirms it.

## Article 8 Quota expansion:

If it is necessary to expand an admission quota under unusual circumstances, the quota expansion shall be proposed to the Committee. The Committee shall convene a meeting to reach a decision and the minutes and relevant documentation shall be submitted to the Committee as well. The quota expansion shall be processed based on the following regulations:

(1) If the expansion of an admission quota is due to the same score, it shall be reported to the MOE within two weeks after the first school day (as stipulated on the school calendar) in the current semester of the academic year wherein the admitted students enroll.

(2) If the expansion of an admission quota is due to any administrative error made by university personnel, an inspection report shall be submitted to the MOE. The admission quota can be expanded upon approval by the MOE.

Article 9 After the application deadline of admission, a department (program, discipline, or division) may choose not to hold its admission examination if the number of applicants applying to the department (program, discipline, or division) is below the minimum number of applicants stipulated by the Committee. In this case, the application fee will be refunded interest-free to all applicants. Also, a department may assist its applicants in applying to another department at the same educational level in a similar field upon approval by the applicants.

Article 10 Examinees may apply for a review of grades or file an appeal within the deadline specified in the admission guidelines if they have any doubts about grading or recruiting affairs which violate their rights and interests. For any unsolvable problem after the processing of personnel in charge of admission affairs, an appeal shall be filed to the Committee with statements and reasons along with documentary evidence within twenty days after the following day of the roll of successful candidates is announced or informed; overdue will not be accepted.

After receiving the appeal, the Committee shall make a reply within a month and advise the appellant of any related administrative remedies. The Committee may form a dedicated taskforce to process the appeal fairly when necessary. Should a conflict of interest arise in the review process among any relevant parties of the Committee meeting, including a Committee member and the appellant, the principle of interest avoidance shall be adopted in accordance with the provisions of Article 32 of “Administrative Procedure Act”.

An appeal shall be filed in writing by the appellant.

The taskforce may, ex officio or upon the appellant’s request, allow the appellant and relevant parties to attend the meeting to give explanations when necessary.

An appellant may file an appeal to the Committee a maximum of once for the same matter. The chairman of the Committee shall inform the appellant in writing of the decision made after a review of the appeal.

Article 11 The Committee shall cautiously handle examination affairs including formulating questions for exams, printing exam papers, producing exam papers, grading exam papers, sealing exam papers, monitoring examinees taking exams, calculating scores, releasing admission results, and registration. The Committee shall also stipulate principles on recusal due to conflicts of interest. Faculty and staff members participating in the examination affairs are obligated to keep the affairs confidential. Anyone who may have a conflict of interest shall avoid being involved in any examination-related tasks, this includes, when:

(1) The examination taker is the examiner himself/herself, his/her spouse, his/her relatives within the third degree, or his/her family member;

(2) Anyone who may have financial or non-financial mutual benefits with a particular examination taker and the relationship may affect the examination results;

(3) Anyone who is employed as a teaching staff at tutorial schools.

All examination and evaluation records and documents shall be stored properly for one year. However, should any appeals be filed according to relevant regulations, the related records and documents shall be kept until the appeal process or the procedures for administrative remedies are

## completed.

Article 12 In the case that the examinees are caught cheating on the exam or the documents presented by examinees found to be forged, counterfeited, borrowing, impersonated or untrue, examinees who haven’t enrolled into the program shall be deprived of their admission qualifications; examinees who have enrolled into the program shall be ordered to withdraw from schooling and no academic records or documents shall be issued. If the situation is discovered after the student has graduated from the University, the diploma shall be revoked; the qualification for graduation shall be invalidated and be publicly announced.

Article 13 The revenue and expenditure of the admission operation for Independent Admission of Students with Excellent Athletic Performance shall be handled pursuant to the University’s regulations governing accounting affairs.

Article 14 Matters not specified herein shall be governed by relevant provisions of the Ministry of Education and the University.

Aeticle15 These regulations will be adopted by Student Recruitment Committee before being reported to the Ministry of Education for ratification and implementation, as shall amendments when they are made.
```

# Yuan Ze University Excellent Student Athletes Reward Rules

2023.3.8 Passed in the 15th Administrative Meeting of the 2022 academic year

## Article 1 Purpose:

Yuan Ze University formulated the "Excellent Student Athletes Reward Rules" (hereinafter referred to as the Rules) to incentivize excellent student athletes to enroll at the University, and to encourage outstanding sports performance as well as active participation in various competitions to enhance the University’s athletic standards and practices.

## Article 2 Reward eligibility:

I. Any student enrolled in accordance with the Ministry of Education’s "Regulations Governing Screening and Examination for Educational Advancement Counseling of Outstanding Student Athletes of Junior High School and Above" or the University’s excellent student athlete enrollment channel shall be rewarded in the first semester of their admission, and may continue to apply for the reward starting from the second semester if they comply with Article 3 of the Counseling Guidelines for Excellent Student Athletes and do not violate Article 5 of the Rules.

II. The preceding paragraph shall also apply to transfer students.

Article 3 Reward: Those who meet the provisions of the preceding article shall be exempted from miscellaneous fees.

Article 4 Application procedures: Those who meet the requirements of Article 2 should apply within the time frame announced each semester. Applicants shall fill out the application form and submit it to the Physical Education Office with the signature and comments of their varsity coach or instructor.

## Article 5 Reward restrictions:

I. Those who apply for the reward in accordance with Article 2 of the Rules shall be disqualified for the reward in the second semester if they have a failing grade in PE or a failing academic grade average in the first semester.

II. Those who apply for the reward in accordance with Article 2 of the Rules shall be disqualified for the reward if they have a failing academic grade average and a conduct grade of under 80 in the previous semester.

III. Those who apply for the reward in accordance with Article 2 of the Rules are required to assist the Office in organizing competitions and activities for 10 hours each semester. These service hours shall be coordinated and determined by the Office at the end of each semester.

IV. Transfer students who apply for the reward in accordance with Article 2 of the Rules must provide proof of admission through the Ministry of Education’s "Regulations Governing Screening and Examination for Educational Advancement Counseling of Outstanding Student Athletes of Junior High School and Above" or the "Independent Admission of Excellent Student Athletes" of their original school.

V. Reward eligibility shall be revoked for students who suspend or terminate their studies or are expelled that semester. Any reward amount issued shall be recovered; eligibility shall not be restored when said students return to school or re-enroll.

VI. If a student who applied for the reward in accordance with Article 2 of the Rules is reported by their coach or instructor as having a poor or lazy attitude in training, or having seriously violated the University's regulations, may have his or her eligibility revoked upon request to relevant committees.

Article 6 Reviewing body: Rewards for excellent student athletes shall be reviewed at the Office Affairs Meetings of the Physical Education Office.

Article 7 Review period: The review meeting will be held after the announced application time in the first and second semester of each academic year.

Article 8 The Rules shall be implemented upon approval from an Administrative Meeting. The same applies to all subsequent amendments.
```

# Yuan Ze University Counseling Guidelines for Excellent Student Athletes

2023.3.8 Passed in the 15th Administrative Meeting of the 2022 academic year

Article 1 Yuan Ze University formulated the Counseling Guidelines for Excellent Student Athletes (hereinafter referred to as the Guidelines) to help excellent student athletes balance schoolwork, life, and training.

Article 2 The term "excellent student athletes" in these Guidelines refers to students who enrolled at the University in accordance with the Ministry of Education’s "Regulations Governing Educational Advancement Counseling of Outstanding Student Athletes of Junior High School and Above" or the University’s excellent student athlete enrollment channel.

Article 3 The responsibilities and obligations of excellent student athletes that the Guidelines apply to are as follows:

I. Excellent student athletes shall participate in varsity team trainings and off-campus training as needed. Absences must be approved by the coach, and an application for leave must be made. Unexplained absences are not allowed. In addition, the number of absent hours per semester shall not exceed one-third of total practice hours.

II. In addition to participating in trainings as stipulated in Subparagraph 1, excellent student athletes must also participate in intercollegiate or national sports competitions organized by the Ministry of Education, the Executive Yuan Sports Affairs Council, or the Chinese Taipei University Sports Federation.

Article 4 The relevant regulations on training, academic, and life counseling for excellent student athletes are as follows:

I. The Office, relevant department head, and class advisor shall reach out and provide counseling for student athletes who received a warning for poor academic performance through the University's "mid-term grade warning system."

II. Academic counseling is arranged by each department according to the University’s Measures for After-School Tutoring.

III. The Office shall arrange a dedicated athletic advisor for each excellent student athlete, to whom students can talk about everyday life and training problems and ask for assistance.

IV. Regular symposiums may be organized by the Office to aid students in addressing their challenges in life, training, and studies, and promote sports injury prevention and treatment. Excellent student athletes must attend at least one symposium every semester.

V. Students experiencing psychological challenges related to their life or academics may be referred to the Academic Affairs Office for professional counseling.

Article 5 The Guidelines have been implemented after approval by an Administrative Meeting. The same shall apply to all subsequent amendments.
```

# Yuan Ze University Sports Injury Prevention and Counseling Guidelines for Excellent Student Athletes

2023.3.8 Passed in the 15th Administrative Meeting of the 2022 academic year

I. Yuan Ze University formulated the Sports Injury Prevention and Counseling Guidelines for Excellent Student Athletes (hereinafter referred to as the Guidelines) to prevent excellent student athletes from getting injured from practicing technical movements during training or between classes.

II. The term "excellent student athletes" in the Guidelines refers to students who enrolled at the University in accordance with the "Regulations Governing Educational Advancement Counseling of Outstanding Student Athletes of Junior High School and Above" or the University’s excellent student athlete enrollment channel.

III. Excellent student athletes participating in training, performances, or pre-game exercises shall be supervised by instructors appointed by their coaches or the Physical Education Office for their safety.

IV. Excellent student athletes are strictly prohibited from practicing high-risk movements on their own after class during the varsity team period. Those who refuse to comply with warnings shall be penalized according to the "Yuan Ze University Varsity Team Management Regulations."

V. Coaches or instructors in each athletic specialty are required to formulate a training plan or exercise prescription to avoid sports injuries caused by overtraining or improper practice methods.

VI. Measures to effectively reduce sports injuries among excellent student athletes and cultivate students' ability to protect themselves are as follows:

(I) Conduct regular sports injury lectures and instruct students on how to prevent and deal with sports injuries.

(II) Have dedicated staff perform regular maintenance of sporting equipment; PE teachers, coaches, and relevant staff shall report any damage to sporting equipment or any safety concerns to the Office before classes or activities.

(III) Accidental injuries shall be handled according to the "Yuan Ze University Emergency Hospital Transport and Escort Measures" formulated by the Health Care Division of the University's Office of Student Affairs.

(IV) The Physical Education Office and Health Care Division shall be equipped with first aid equipment and supplies for treating accident sports injuries, and replenish supplies as needed.

(V) Provide information on hospitals contracted by the University to help students handle sports injuries.

VII. Those who wish to participate in competitions, off-campus training, or on-campus winter or summer training must first submit an application to the Office, and may only participate in said competitions or trainings once their application is approved.

VIII. The Guidelines have been implemented after approval by an Administrative Meeting. The same shall apply to all subsequent amendments.
```

<!-- OCR_END -->

- **64. [超連結（檔案）]**: files/regulations/c%20en/1-94.pdf

```markdown
# Yuan Ze University Guidelines Governing Academic Grading

Passed by the 4th Academic Affairs Meeting of the 2022 School Year, March 1, 2023

Passed by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting of the 2024 School Year, April 23, 2025

## Article 1 Yuan Ze University Guidelines Governing Academic Grading are formulated to process the affairs of academic grading.

## Article2

Course instructors shall upload all grades to the online grade submission system within the designated time limit specified in the academic calendar for each academic year. In order not to hinder students' rights concerning their further studies, employment, scholarship application, change of majors, minor studies, or double majors, instructors who have not turned in students’ grades by the deadline shall be notified by the Office of Academic Affairs to expedite the process. The department offering the course shall also be notified to assist with expediting the process. If a student is unable to obtain their final exam results due to certain circumstances, resulting in the instructor's inability to upload the grades, the instructor shall submit a written request in advance with an explanation for the delay in submitting the grades and an estimated date for the resubmission of the grades. The resubmission of grades shall be completed no later than the final exam of the following semester. Upon approval of the Academic Dean can the delay of grade submission be allowed.

Article 3 All instructors shall preserve students’ midterm and final exam papers, term projects or reports for one semester since the end of the current semester. The preserved term papers and reports will be references once any dispute over grades occurs.

If it is necessary to change a student’s grade after being uploaded to the online grade submission system, the instructor shall submit a written request along with relevant supporting documentation. Upon approval from the department chairman or office director, the process will be carried out according to the following procedures:

1. If the change of grade does not involve the change of status of passing or failing a course, the grade can be changed upon approval of the Academic Dean.

2. If the change of grade involves the change of status of passing or failing a course, the grade can be changed after the change isdiscussed and passed by the Academic Affairs Meeting which the instructor shall attend to provide an explanation.

3. If an application for changing a grade requires review by the Academic

Affairs Meeting, it shall be submitted no later than the convening of the first Academic Affairs Meeting of the following semester. If the whole process of grade correction completes at a time that has passed the beginning of the ranking process, reranking will not be permissible (except for graduation rankings), in order not to hinder other students’ rights,

## Article 4

Rankings of grades are divided into the following types according to classes, departments (majors, groups (not include the grouping of students based on their enrollment statuses)):

1. Semester grade ranking: indicates the average semester grade ranking of a student who engaged in studies during the semester.

2. Academic year grade ranking: indicates the average grade ranking of two semesters of a student who engaged in studies during the academic year.

3. Grade ranking of each year of the previous studies: indicates the rank of all the grades from previous semesters since the beginning of the one’s studies.

4. Graduates’ grade ranking: indicates the average previous semesters grades of those who graduated in the same year.

## Article 5

Retaking a course that has already been passed is limited to one time, and both grades will be recorded on the transcript (i.e., the same course will appear twice with separate grades). Both grades will be included in the calculation of the graduation GPA; however, only one set of credits will be counted toward graduation requirements..

Article 6 Matters not specified herein shall be governed by “Yuan Ze University Study Regulations” and other relevant provisions.

Article 7 These regulations will be adopted by Academic Affairs Meeting before ratification and implementation, as shall amendments when they are made.
```
